@001

#, ,DRIN CAN RTZA BA'I BLA MA NGAG DBANG BLO BZANG RGYA MTSO'I
THUN MONG

PHYI'I RNAM THAR DU K'U LA'I GOS BZANG GLEGS BAM

BZHI PA'I 'PHROS LNGA PA BZHUGS,

RAB BYUNG BCU GCIG PA'I CHU PHAG LO'I NANG SHEL DKAR MI 'GYUR
RDO RJE RDZONG DU

RGYAL BA'I BKA' 'GYUR GSAR BZHENGS GNANG BA SOGS KYI SKOR,

*, ,KHRAGo SKYUGo CESo PAo CHU PHAG LO'Io GNAMo LOo GSARo TSESo
KYIo SRID GSUM BDAG MO MCHOD

PA'I DUS STON GTOR MA BYIN RLABS NAS BZUNG NGOS PHEBS MA GNANG
BA LAS SNGAR RGYUN BZHIN DANG,

BSTAN SKYONG TSOGS 'KHOR 'GYED PA'I GRAL BYINGS KHAMS GSUM DANG,
GZIMS CHUNG NANG DU NGED,

BSTAN 'DZIN D'A LAS RGYAL PO, SE CHEN DBON PO, BCAR BZHUGS ZHABS
PHYI NANG SKOR SOGS DANG, DRUNG

'KHOR BYINGS SOGS KHAMS GSUM 'GAG TU BSGRIGS, DGUNG TSIGS THOG
TSOMS CHEN DU NGED DANG

BSTAN 'DZIN D'A LAS KHANG SOGS RGYAL KHAG ,CHOS SDE KHAG PHAN
TSUN SOGS KYI MKHAN SLOB, LAS SNE BA,

RGYUN BZHUGS DRUNG 'KHOR SER MO BA, PHYOGS MTHA'I LO GSAR 'BUL
MI BCAS PA BZHUGS GRAL DGA'

STON GAR ROL, RNAM GLING PAn CHEN DANG LHA KHANG PA RDO RJE NOR
BUS GRAL 'PHROS SOGS SNGAR RGYUN BZHIN

BZAB RGYAS SU BSTAR, TSESo GNYISo LAo GRAL SNGA MA LTA BU NAS
RAGS BSDUS THOG RNAM PAR RGYAL BA'I PHAN

BDE LEGS BSHAD GLING (2NA) GRA TSANG YONGS RDZOGS, RIN CHEN
RGYAN CHA BA SUM CU SKOR, BKRA SHIS

RTAGS RDZAS 'BUL MI GRA TSANG GI GSUNG BZANG BA SOGS SNGAR RGYUN
BZHIN BYIN CHAGS PA LA GONG GI RTAGS

RDZAS SOGS TSIG DANG BSTUN 'BUL BA'I STANG KHA'I GONG GI DE
GZIMS CHUNG DU PHUL ZHING TSAR GCIG NGED LA

@002

SPRAD, MCHOD SPRIN SNA BRGYAD KYI ZLOS GAR SOGS DGA' STON RGYAS
PAR BSTAR RO,,

GNYIS (RIGS PA'I RGYU RGYAN,) LDAN 'BYUNG BA KHRAGo SKYUGo GNAMo
LOo YI, ,YID 'ONG ZLA BA DAG PA'I 'DZUM

BSTAN TSE, ,SRIDo PA GSUMo GYI BDAGo MOo LEGS BSNYEN PA'I, ,RDO
RJE RI RAB RJES 'GRO'I MCHOD GTOR

DANG, ,LHA MI'I (DGA' BA'I NYAMS LDAN,) SGEGS PA BKRA SHIS DNGOS
PO BYE BA 'BUM, ,NYAMS BRGYAS RNAM SGEG

ZLOS PA'I GAR STABS STONG, ,'DOD YON STONG KHUN MING DU ZAD BYED
PA'I, ,YA RABS BZANG PO'I SROL

DU BTOD 'DI RANGS, ,ZHES BAR SKABS KYI TSIGS SU BCAD PA'O,,

TSESo LNGAo LAo BYA KHYUNG CHOS RJE KHRI PA'I 'BUL BA DANG, THOR
GOD AA YU shI'I 'BUL BA BTEG ,'DI

(2BA) LO SMON LAM TSUGS NAS ZHAG BCO LNGA'I BAR DGONGS PA CHOS
DBYINGS SU RDZOGS THABS DGONGS

JA RE 'THOL LA RJEo BLAo MAo SRIDo ZHI'Io GTZUGo RGYANo GYI SKU
RIM DU BTAGS PA'I PHUNG PO GSUM PA DANG, MANG

JA GZHAN LA GDUGS DKAR GANG 'GRO, LUG DRUG CU RE BDUN GYI SROG
BLU, GSER ZHO NYI SHU'I GSER

GSOL DANG BRGYA MCHOD, SOG PO DBUL NGES DANG MU TO BAR SBYIN
GTONG, TSESo BCUo GCIGo LA MTSO SNA

RDZONG SDONG RONG GRAGS PA BA'I TSAB RGYA LEGS PA PHUN TSOGS
RNAM RGYAL RDZONG BDA' BYAS, TSESo BCOo LNGAo LAo

MAR KHAL BRGYA LNGA BCU'I DKAR ME SOGS BRGYA MCHOD TSAR BCU, NA
BZA' SPONG THAG TU KHA G-YAR GYIS LHA

SA SMON LAM CHEN MO'I TSOGS SU GRA PA RER DNGUL ZHO PHYED DO
MA'I RTZIS LA ZHAL DKAR LEGS PA GNYIS,

DNGUL GYI DKAR STEGS GNYIS, BZED ZHAL GNYIS, CHAB RIL RGYAN DRUG
MA GNYIS, DNGUL MDONG

GNYIS, DNGUL LTIR CHUNG BA GCIG ,THA PHAG GSUM, DBU PAn MU TIG
GI RGYAN YOD GCIG ,HOR JUS

GZHI LU'I SKU BER GCIG ,GOS SKYER GYI SKU BER MU TIG GI RGYAN
YOD GCIG ,BER DKYUS MA DRUG ,SKU

'GAN SBYAR LNGA, SKU CHOS BCU, SKU MTHANG BCU GCIG ,TZAR MO BCU
GCIG ,SKU 'GAG BZHI, SKU G-YOGS

,ZHABS PHYAGS BCU GNYIS, KHA

MA BCU (3NA) DGU, SBUG CHOL GSUM, SIL SNYAN GSUM, DRIL BU RDOR

@003

GYI GOS YOL BCU GNYIS, SGA RA MA LUG NYI SHU RTZA DGU ,SGA DMAR
NYI SHU RTZA DRUG ,CHIBS CHEN GNYIS

RNAMS KYI RI GONG KHYON BSDOMS PAR DNGUL SRANG STONG PHRAG GCIG
DANG SUM BRGYA ZHE BZHI'I RTZIS, 'DI LO

SMON LAM DU 'GRUL PA SOGS KYI PHYI 'GYED BCU GCIG DANG, RJEo
BLAo MA'Io NA BZA' SPONG THAG TU MI

GTOGS PA'I MI RER DNGUL ZHO RE'I RTZIS RTA RMIG MA'I 'GYED, BUR
'GYED GCIG BCAS DGONGS RDZOGS

SU DMIGS PA SONG, NGEDo RANGo GI RIM GROR MANG JA GNYIS LA SHER
SNYING DANG SROG BLU SO GCIG ,BRTAG

BSGRIL DANG GTZUG LAG SKOR GYI MO PHY'A, CHOS SKYONG LE TSAN GYI
GSUNG BCAS, GZHAN YANG SKU RIM DU KHA

G-YAR BA'I DGONGSo PAo RDZOGSo THABSo DANG, MYUR PHEBS KYI CHED
'BA' ZHIG YIN YANG SGRIB SHING LUGS

PHRAN BU BCAS 'PHYONG RGYAS, RIN SPUNGS, PA SNAM, GZHI RTZE,
NGAM RING, GTING SKYES, SKU RAB RNAM RGYAL,

RGYA MDA', RTZE SGANG, ZHO KHA, SKYEM SPRAG LUNG, SOG TZAN DAN
DGON, MDZO SGANG, 'BA', RGYAL RTZE, LHA SA,

CHU SHUR, GONG DKAR, DO RDZONG, PHO BRANG BCAS RDZONG GZHIS NYI
SHU RTZA GCIG TU, BKA' 'GYUR, SMAN BLA,

YIG DRUG ,GSANG SNGAGS GSAR RNYING GI TSE SGRUB, LHA SA, RA MO
CHE, YER PA, KA TSAL, CHU BO RI, BSAM

YAS, YANG RDZONG, MCHIMS PHU, GNAM LCAGS BRAG ,(3BA) 'ON BU STAG
TSANG, BYA SA, KHRA 'BRUG ,BU

CHU, PHUNG PO RI BO CHE, G-YUNG PHU RDZA LHUD, ZAM BU LUNG,
GTZANG 'GRAM, GROM PA RGYANG, RI BO BKRA BZANG,

PRA DUN TZE, MKHO MTHING, MKHAR CHU, MON KHA SENG GE RDZONG SOGS
GNAS CHEN NYI SHU RTZA GSUM DU TSE CHOG,

GTOR BZLOG ,TSOGS BRGYA, ME MCHOD SOGS, CHOS 'KHOR RGYAL DU LHA
MO SOGS CHOS SRUNG TSOR BSKANG

BA 'BUM THER DANG, GZHAN MA TSOR KHRI TSAR, RTZED THANG BSAM
GTAN GLING, 'PHAN YUL DPAL LDAN RTZE,

SA SKYA MGON KHANG, KHA'U SKYES LHAS, RIN CHEN SGANG MGON KHANG
RNAMS SU MGON PO CHE CHUNG LAS MKHAN

DANG BCAS PA, BRAG RAM DU BEG TZE, BO DONG AER DMAG ZOR MA BCAS
PA BSKANG GSO, MAL GRO GZI

CHEN, KLU SBUG ,KLU RGYAL RNAMS LA KLU GTA' KLU BCOS KLU RTEN
KLU GTOR BCAS KHYON BSDOMS BKA'

@004

GZUNGS RING SUM STONG BDUN BRGYA LNGA BCU, DE'I SNYING PO NYIS
STONG NYIS BRGYA, NYE SNYING CHIG KHRI CHIG STONG

NYIS BRGYA, MI 'KHRUGS PA'I BDAG MDUN BUM SGRUB DANG 'BREL BA'I
GZUNGS BYE BA GNYIS SA YA GNYIS

BDUN 'BUM BRGYAD KHRI BDUN STONG, BUM SGRUB DANG 'BREL PA'I YIG
BRGYA SA YA BRGYAD DRUG 'BUM SUM

KHRI CHIG STONG, AA MA RA nI CHIG KHRI (4NA) BRGYAD STONG BDUN
BRGYA, TSE GZUNGS SA YA DRUG DANG DRUG 'BUM

DRUG KHRI SUM STONG BRGYAD BRGYA LNGA BCU, SGROL GZUNGS SUM KHRI
SUM STONG BDUN BRGYA, NYA'I SROG BLU SUM

'BUM, SMAN BLA SUM KHRI BDUN STONG DRUG BRGYA DRUG CU, RIL SGRUB
DANG 'BREL BA'I YIG DRUG DUNG PHYUR

BZHI DANG SA YA BZHI SUM 'BUM LNGA KHRI, MCHOD PA, KHRUS GSOL
SUM STONG, GTOR MA BRGYA RTZA CHIG

'BUM DRUG KHRI DGU STONG BRGYAD BRGYA, LTUNG BSHAGS CHIG KHRI
DGU STONG BRGYAD CU, BLA MA GSANG 'DUS KYI

SNYING PO BYE BA GNYIS DANG SA YA BZHI DGU 'BUM SUM KHRI LNGA
STONG CHIG BRGYA BCO BRGYAD, BSAM PA LHUN

GRUB MA DGU STONG, GDUGS DKAR BDUN KHRI DRUG STONG DRUG BRGYA,
SHER SNYING CHIG 'BUM BZHI KHRI SUM

STONG DRUG BRGYA BZHI BCU, SGROL MA CHIG 'BUM DGU KHRI NYIS
STONG BDUN BRGYA BZHI BCU, ZHABS BRTAN

SUM STONG LNGA BRGYA, PO TA LAR GRA TSANG YONGS RDZOGS KYI RNAM
'JOMS KYI GZUNGS CHOG DANG 'BREL BA

TSES BZHI NAS BDUN GSUM GYI BAR TSUGS PAR GZUNGS RING BZHI 'BUM
BDUN STONG DRUG BRGYA LHAG

TZAM DANG, YANG SNYING SA YA GCIG KHRI TSO BRGYAD LNGA STONG
LNGA BRGYA DRUG CU, MTHA' 'DUL YANG 'DUL RU

GNON SOGS GNAS CHEN RNAMS SU TSES BRGYAD, BCU, BCO LNGA, NYER
LNGA, GNAM GANG BCAS KYI DUS

BZANG THOG ZHAL GSER SPYAN 'BYED, MCHOD PA SNA LNGA, SNYAN DAR
GRANGS BZHI RES NYUNG MTHA' BYAS PA'I

SPYAN 'DREN KHRUS GSOL YAN LAG (4BA) BDUN PA, SKYABS SEMS RNAMS
'GRO GANG CHE, MI SER SPYI LA

YUL 'GYED DANG JA RE'I THOG MA nI DANG DMIGS BRTZE MA, RIS MED
DGON AANG DANG GNYIS GSUM GA LA

'GYED DANG, MANG JA SBYOR SBREL THOG GDUGS DKAR SHER SNYING
SGROL MA, DGE DGON RNAMS LA JA RE

'THOL BTANG BA'I DMIGS BRTZE MA, RNYING LUGS RNAMS LA JA RE'I
'THOL THOG BSAM PA LHUN GRUB MA,

NGEDo KYIo RIMo GRORo RIN SPUNGS SOGS RDZONG GZHIS KHAG BCO
LNGAR BKA' 'GYUR SOGS DANG, MCHIMS BU,

@005

YANG RDZONG, SHEL BRAG GSUM DU TSOGS BRGYA DANG ME MCHOD, DVAGS
GRA TSANG GIS MA nI DUNG PHYUR, MNGA'

RIS GRA TSANG PAS GDUGS DKAR 'BUM THER, BYANG CHUB GLING PAS
AAY'EE RING DANG, YANG BZLOG RDO RJE PHA

LAM BYE CHUNG RE, THANG SAG PAS BZANG SPYOD 'BUM THER, GONG DKAR
DU PHY'A PHRIN NOR BU MCHOG RGYAS KYI

G-YANG 'GUGS, SHEL BRAG TU DGRA MNAN BDUN GCIG DANG, LHA SAR
RNAM RGYAL GRA TSANG GI GRA PA GRANGS

BCAD KYIS RGYAL PO RTZE MDOS SNGAR RGYUN BZHIN RGYAS PAR BSTAR,
GZHAN MA RNAMS KHYON BSDOMS BKA'

'GYUR TSAR BRGYA DANG BRGYAD, 'BUM BRGYA DANG DRUG ,BRGYAD STONG
PA DRUG ,NYI KHRI LNGA, BSKAL BZANG GCIG,

GSER 'OD CHIG STONG, BKA' THANG CHIG STONG, GDUGS DKAR DGU 'BUM
DGU KHRI BDUN BRGYA, SHER

SNYING DGU KHRI, SGROL MA BDUN 'BUM BRGYAD KHRI, TSE GZUNGS DGU
KHRI RNAMS, BSTANo SRIDo SPYI RIM DU RDZONG

GZHIS GNAS CHEN (5NA) BSDOMS PA KHYON BCU DGUR MDOS GTOR DGRA
MNAN, DGRA LHA DPANGS

BSTOD, DRAG PO'I SBYIN SREG ,BODo KHAMSo SPYI RIM DU YUL GRU SO
SO NAS BKA' 'GYUR SOGS DANG, GONG

DKAR DU DUNG DGON PA BAS MA MO GLENG GZHI DANG, SRID PA SPYI
MDOS, ZHOL DU ZHANG STON PAS KLU BCOS,

RTZER RNAM RGYAL GRA TSANG NAS BSTAN MDOS RNAMS SMIN RGYAS,

ZLAo BAo GNYISo PA'Io TSESo DRUGo LAo CHOS RJE BCO BRGYAD PAS
ZHUS NGOR GDAN SA 'OG KHRI CHEN 'JAM

DBYANGS TSE DBANG RIG 'DZIN BKRA SHIS DANG, 'JAM DBYANGS NGAG
DBANG NOR BU GNYIS KYI BRTAN

BZHUGS, BSAM YAS SU DGE SLONG 'JAM DBYANGS GRAGS PA, THANG PO
CHE DANG TSONG 'DUS SU LKOG PA

PHUN TSOGS DBANG PO, LA MOR CHANG KHYIM NGAG DBANG MKHYEN BRTZE
BCAS THON PA'I BSAM YAS SU GNOD

SBYIN TZE'U DMAR PO DANG, TSONG 'DUS SU BYA KHRID MIG GCIG PAR
CHAB SHOG SNYAN TSIG GI LAM NAS DRANGS

PA'I TSUL, THANG CHEN GYIS NA NING GI DRI BA'I DUS SOGS MA RTOGS
KYANG, RJES SU 'PHYONG RGYAS KHUL LA ZHI

NAS DOGS PA MANG BA BYUNG 'DUG PAS YIN NAM RTING SOR SKU MI
PHEBS PA SOGS GNANG SGO DOGS PA

YOD PA MDZAD 'DUG PA SOGS DANG BCAS DE RIGS MDZAD NA MI YONG
GSOL ZHING TSONG 'DUS SOGS LHA

'DRE DMANGS NAS DON MA RTOGS 'DUG PA'I KUN RDZOB SHA STAG DANG,
DE GONG NAS SKU PHEBS LO RER

@006

ZANGS RI SDE SRID KYIS 'GAN BZHES DUS NYUNG MTHA' DRUG BDUN RE
DANG, DE TSUN YANG GNYIS GSUM

(5BA) RE GNANG GI YOD PAS THANG CHEN SKU PHEBS DGOS LUGS DANG
BCAS LKOG PA BTANG BA'I RGYAL

KHAMS LO PHYUGS SOGS SBOM CHAR GYI DRI BA ZHUS SO,,

MTHU STOBS RTZE BRGYAS RGOL (BSDUS PA'I GZUGS CAN,) NGAN SBYIN
SKYES KYI, ,DPUNG PA 'JOMS DPA'

THANGo CHENo YONo TANo RGYALo, ,DUS GSUM GZIGS PA'I SGRIB MED YE
SHES KYIS, ,SNANG TSUL YID GNYIS

RTAGS MDZAD RGYU MTSAN DBUL, ,ZHES BAR SKABS KYI TSIGS SU BCAD
PA'O,,

BSAM YAS SU GTZUG LAG KHANG DU SMON 'DEBS DANG CHOS SKYONG TZI'U
DMAR BAS KYANG RDO RJE BRAG

RIG 'DZIN SPRUL PA'I SKUR KHYI PHAG RGYAL PO'I BANG CHEN SOGS
KYIS MTSON GSANG BRTOL DU NYE BA'I GNANG

SGO JI SNYED GCIG BYUNG ZHING, SNGA LO PADMA'I RIGS SOGS LUNG
BSTAN YANG MDZAD PA BCAS GNOD SBYIN CHEN

PO GNANG LUGS RES 'DRA BAR DES NA GONG NAS BSTEN MCHOD GNANG
BAR, LAR RGYAR GANG GNOD MDZAD

PA SOGS BLOR MA RAN PA BCAS RE GNYIS KYIS ZHI BAS LAB PA LAS
DRAG 'JUN MI 'GAB ZER YANG, ZHI

DRAG DU MA'I SGO NAS GSANG BRTOL MDZAD NA YE SHES PA'I CHOS
SKYONG DON DU GA NAS YIN, YIN NA BSTEN

MCHOD BYAS PAS LAR RGYAR GNOD PA DANG BCAS MIN THAG CHOD CING,
YE SHES PA NI NAM DU'ANG BRTEN SKU

KHOG SOGS GANG BYED NGED LA DBANG BA YIN SOGS YIG NGAG GI SGO
NAS GSANG BRTOL MI MDZAD PA'I

DAM 'DOGS, SPRUL PA'I SKU GAR PHEBS KYI DBUS DRI MAL KYANG MANG
TZAM BGYIS PAR, LO MO SNGA LO LUNG

BSTAN PAR MA 'DUS PA MED, SNGAR PHAN 'DRES GANG (6NA) DU BLTA
BAR PHYIN KYANG MNGAL DU YOD SHAS NI

KHA, BTZAS PA NI MA MTHONG AANG, ZHES DANG, BRDA TSIG TZAM MA
BYAS NA MI YONG BA LAS SLAR NAS MI

MDZAD PA'I ZHAL DAN MDZAD DO,,

BRGYUD LDAN BLA MA'I (BYA BA BRJOD PA BAR GYI GSAL, BYED) DAM
TSIG RDO RJE'I RGYA, ,GTZUG BKOD BSTAN SRUNG

GTZOR GYUR TZE'U DMARo (BSAM YAS,) BAo, ,YE SHES LHA LA KUN RTOG
'KHRUL RJES SU, ,'BRENG BA'I RNYOG PA'I DRI

MA RING BTANG YANG, ,GZHAN (YON TAN RANG BZHIN BRJOD,) RKYEN
DBANG GIS GZUGS CAN KHOG BRLAMS TSE, ,MI

@007

SRUN ROL GAR SNA TSOGS STON PA LA, ,SNGON GYI G-YAR DAM BSGRAGS
PA'I THA TSIG GIS, ,TSUL BZHIN

'PHRIN LAS SGRUB PAR ZHAL GYIS 'CHES, ,BSTAN (MTSUNGS GSAL,) DPE
PA RIN CHEN GANG NA GNAS PA LA,,

MTHU LDAN RDO RJE'I SRUNG MA JI SNYED PA, ,PADMA'I MTSO LA BUNG
BA 'DU BA BZHIN, ,SRUNG SKYOB MI G-YEL MDZAD

LAS KHYAD PAR DU, ,TSANGSo (RAB BRTAGS PA,) LHAo YIo MEo TOGo
SRAS BCAS KYIS, ,SNGON NAS ZANo G-YANGo GTZUG

LAG KHANG CHEN PO'I, ,GNYER DU BSKOS NAS DAM TSIG GCIG SBREL
BA'I, ,'DA' DKA'I DAM TSIG GCIG

TU DGONGS PA 'DRA, ,ZHES BAR SKABS KYI TSIGS SU BCAD PA'O,,

LA MOR DE MTSUNGS PHEBS GRUB MA GRUB KYI DRI BA DANG BAR DU LUNG
BSTAN MI GNANG BA NA NING DON

DER DGONGS NA SNGAR YANG MA 'ONGS LUNG BSTAN MANG BA DANG, PHYI
MA GNANG BAR YUN SONG BA BCAS MA

'ONGS LUNG BSTAN DGOS TSUL ZHUS PAR, CHANG KHYIM PA RANG GIS YIG
MKHAN BYAS NAS (6BA) 'PHRAL DU

GNANG 'DUG PA'I NANG, GZHAN G-YO 'GUL YONG BA GA LA SRID, CES PA
NAS, ,GNAS SA 'DZIN DBANG

PO'I RTZE MO NAS, ,SKYABS THUGS RJE'I 'OD ZER PHYOGS BCUR 'PHRO,
,MA SEMS CAN SDUG BSNGAL

'JIGS LAS GROL, ,SGOS LHA MI'I RE BA SKONG BAS BZANG, ,DGE BSTAN
PA'I GZHI 'DZIN GNAS MCHOG

RGYAL, ,LHA SRID GSUM BDAG MO DMAG ZOR MAS, ,LAS RNAM BZHI'I
'JA' TSON GUR PHUB CING, ,MA SHA

ZA MKHA' 'GRO BRAN BKOL NAS, ,'KHOR DUS BZHI LHA MOS LAS RNAMS
SGRUB, ,SHEL MCHONG LTAR SMUG

PA'I 'DAB BRGYA'I GLING, ,DER SNA TSOGS RDO RJE'I LTE BA'I DBUS,
,SENG MTHU LDAN GNAS MAL 'CHA' BA

LA, ,ZER NYI MA'I 'OD KYANG DE LA 'KHOR, ,SENG GANGS LA MOS PA'I
KHA RLANGS KYI, ,SHAR RGYA MTSO'I MGRON

'GUGS MTHAR YANG KHYAB, ,CES PA RNAMS ZHING GZHAN DU GSHEGS PA
DANG MCHOG GI SPRUL SKU PHEBS PA'I

SKOR YIN 'DUG PAS PHYIR SGRAGS NA MI GO BA CAN GYIS RTOGS DOGS
'DUG ZHUS PA'I 'DIR GONG

GSAL SOGS TSANG MA DAM 'BYAR GCIG DANG BYINGS LA TSIG 'DI RNAMS
MED PA DANG, DAM 'BYAR GCIG

LA MO RANG DU BZHAG 'DUG PA LAS 'DI SKABS LUNG BSTAN GZHAN MA
PHEBS YUL SOGS LA CHER MA

@008

THAMS CAD MKHYEN PA PADM'A KAo RAo (YON TAN RANG BZHIN BRJOD
PA,) YIS, ,DREGS PA YONGS KYI RJE BOR DBANG

BSKUR BA'I, ,MTHU LDAN DGEo (LA MO,) BSNYEN CHEN PO BKRA SHIS
DUNG, ,G-YAS 'DZUM CODo PANo 'CHANG BAS

YONGS GRAGS DANG, ,KUN (CHOS DPE,) GYIS MA RTOGS (7NA) MA 'ONGS
BZANG NGAN BAR, ,BDE SDUG ZA 'OG

RNAM BKRA'I THAGS BZHIN DU, ,CI YANG 'CHAR BA LAG MTHIL SKYU RU
RA'I, ,DNGOS PO JI BZHIN BSTAN PA'ANG

MTSAR DU CHE, ,ZHES BAR SKABS KYI TSIGS SU BCAD PA'O,,

SPAG SHOD KHANG GSAR BKRA SHIS RAB BRTAN GRA DMANGS RNAMS KYIS
ZHUS NGOR RTA TSAG RJE DRUNG

NGAG DBANG DKON COG NYI MA'I 'KHRUNGS RABS DANG 'BREL BA'I BRTAN
BZHUGS BKA' RTZOM TSUL DU

SONG, NYERo BZHIo LAo NGAM RING BSAM GRUB DGA' LDAN GYI BLA MAR
BDE YANGS DBU MDZAD NGAG DBANG

STOBS LDAN DANG, SHA BUM BLA MAR RIN CHEN BRAG BLA MA 'PHAGS
MCHOG RNAM RGYAL GYI NYIS LCOGS SU RDZONG

BDA' BYAS, NYERo LNGAo LAo RJEo BLAo MAo SRIDo ZHI'Io GTZUGo
RGYANo GYI DGONGS RDZOGS SKU MCHOD DU LHA SA RA MO CHE

DMAR LCAGS BCAS PAR RGYA MCHOD DANG SER 'BRAS SU ZHABS BRTAN DU
KHA G-YAR BA'I NA BZA' SPONG

DAG LUGS DGE 'DUN RER DNGUL ZHO RE'I RTZIS 'DI LO NAS RGYUN
BTZUGS BYAS SO,,

NYON MONGS (MTHA' DAG GZUGS CAN,) DRI MA BRAL BA'I BSIL SBYIN
MKHAN, ,RNAM MKHYEN CHA SHAS

RDZOGS PA'I RANG BZHIN MOD, ,MA DAG GDUL BYA'I NGO BOR 'PHEL
'GRIB TSUL, ,CUNG ZAD STON PA'I DRI

DAG DANG MA DAG RIGS, MA YONGS GZHIL SLAD, ,'PHRULo BYA BA RANG
BZHIN BRJOD, SNANGo DMAR LCAGS RA MO CHE BCAS

PA'I, ,RTEN DU RGYA MCHOD NA BZA' SPONG DAG TSUL, ,SER 'BRAS
NYER MTSON 'KHOR GSUM YONGS SU DAG

PA YI, ,RIN THANG GZHAL DU MED PA'I DNGOS PO'I SGO, RIG GROL
MCHOG GYUR (7BA) DGEo 'DUN BGRANG

YAS (TING NGE 'DZIN DANG 'BREL BA'I PHUL BYUNG,) PAR, ,GZHAN
PHAN GTER RGYA GROL BAS JI SRID BAR, ,RAB PHYE

GTAN PA MED PA'I MCHOD SBYIN GYIS, ,DPAG BSAM SHING YANG SMRA
BCAD ZOL LA BKOD, ,CES BAR

SKABS KYI TSIGS SU BCAD PA'O,,

SKU RAB DGA' LDAN RAB BRTAN PAR 'BYED KHRAR MA GSAL BA'I THUGS
BZOS RU'I KHAL LNGA BCU

@009

NGA GNYIS DANG BRE BZHI PHUL PHYED BZHI, RTZA RI AU RI BAR BRE

BAR SHAS ZHING SON RU'I KHAL GSUM 'GRO BA RNAMS 'JAGS 'OS MA CHE
YANG DGE 'DUN DU BSAMS

STON MO, CHOS 'KHOR RGYAL GYI ZHABS

BRTAN 'BUL MI RNAMS KYIS SGROL MA BRGYAD KHRI BZHI STONG RNAMS
SONG, NYIo SHUo LNGAo RJESo MARo THUGS SRAS

DMIGS PA'I LO MTSAMS ZHIG MDZAD

RGYUR THUN MTSAMS ZHAL 'DON DU ZHUS PA'I BRTAN BZHUGS SMON LAM
BKA' RTZOM GYI TSUL DU SONG,

TSES GSUM NAS NYIN BDUN GYI BAR MYUR PHEBS LA DMIGS RNAM RGYAL
GRA TSANG YONGS RDZOGS KYIS

SKONGS BSHAGS DANG 'BREL BA'I LHA MO'I SGER BSKANG CHIG 'BUM
CHIG KHRI NYIS BRGYA GNYIS DANG, LCAM

SRING GI BSKANG BA BZHI STONG CHIG BRGYA BZHI BCU, SPYIR BSKANG
NYIS BRGYA LNGA BCU RNAMS, RMI LAM DU BEG

TZE'I BSKANG BA DGOS 'DRA SNYAM PA'I MTSAN MA ZHIG BYUNG DON
BZHIN DU BEG TZER 'PHRIN BCOL GSAR

'DZUGS DANG BCAS RGYAL DU BSKANG BA 'BUM THER, DMAG ZOR MAR
KHRI, GZHAN RNAMS LA STONG RTZA, SNYAN

DAR DANG BCAS PA BSTAR, ZLA BA GNYIS PA'I TSES BCU GCIG DANG,
GSUM PA RJES MA'I TSES BCO

BRGYAD LA RLUNG CHE BA, GTZUG LAG LTAR NA MIG DMAR SOGS DRAG
GZA' RLUNG SKAR GYI STENG DU PHYIR LOG

NAG SOGS TSANG MAR SNGON MA DE BYUNG

'DUG PAS BOD GCIG PUR MA ZAD SEMS CAN KUN LA MI BDE BA'I RTAGS
LAS SGER DOGS MA DGOS

KYANG, RLUNG GI BZLOG THABS LA KHAG BTAGS KYIS MYURo PHEBSo SOGS
LA DBUS GTZANG DANG KHAMS KYI

'BAL 'BAL RANG LUS SROG RGYU NOR LA SKYON 

@041

MED NGOS SA RIGS GZHUNG LEN BYAS PA'I LTO SKAL DU YUL SNGA LCAGS
RI BA'I KHANG PA LAG 'DEBS 'BRU

KHAL BRGYA NYI SHU SKOR THON PA, DUD CHUNG GCIG GI MI GRA DANG
BCAS PA BYIN ZHING, BUR YANG DGONGS

RDZOGS SU BSAMS BRJOD MED DU BZHAG,

ZLAo BAo DGUo PA'Io TSESo GNYISo LAo RATNA'I SPYI LUNG LAS CHOS
SDE BCU GSUM 'CA' BAR LUNG BSTAN

PA'I GRA, KAR LUGS DGE TSAL BA 'PHO BSKYAS KYI SHUL DU RJEo BLAo
MAo SRID (32BA) ZHI'Io GTZUGo RGYANo MCHOG

GIS SA SKYONG BSOD NAMS RAB BRTAN DU BSLABS STON GNANG BA'I
RNYING PA'I GRA SON MED PAR LCAGS YOS

GRA KHRAL GSAR RGYAG SOGS BTZUGS PA'I THOSo BSAMo DARo RGYASo
GLING BLA MA, GRA DMANGS NYIS BRGYA SKOR

GYI 'BUL BA BTEG STE ZHABS BRTAN PHUL, AU CHING TSOGS GSOG DAR
RGAN RAB 'BYAMS PAS DGA'

LDAN BSTAN 'DZIN BO SHOG THU RGYAL PO'I BSTAN JUS RGYAS PHYIR
CHOS 'KHOR RGYAL DU SNYAN DAR PHUL BA'I KHA

BYANG, MCHOD DPON NGAG DBANG SHES RAB ROGS BCAS RGYAL DU DNGUL
GDUNG GZUNGS 'BUL LA RDZONG

BDA' BYAS SKABS BYAMS CHEN DANG, LHA MOR 'BUL RGYU'I SNYAN DAR
KHA BYANG, RNAM RGYAL GRA TSANG DGE

BSKOS BLO GROS RNAM RGYAL GYIS 'JOG TU DNGUL SRANG BCU BZHI'I
PAD SDER PHUL BA'I KHA BYANG, BE RI RAB

'BYAMS PA NGAG DBANG LEGS PAS ZHUS NGOR BRTAN BZHUGS SMON LAM
RNAMS BKA' RTZOM TSUL DU BYAS,

TSESo GSUMo LAo DGA' LDAN BSTAN 'DZIN BO SHOG THU KHANG GIS TSE
DPAG MED KYI DNGUL SKU GSAR

BZHENGS LNGA BCU DANG NA BZA' SKOR, DNGUL LNGA BCU MA SOGS 'BUL
DPANGS MTHO BA DANG, RNAM RGYAL

GRA TSANG DU DNGUL LTIR TSA GSER MA DGU, YON 'GYED TSOGS 'KHOR
SOGS RGYA CHER SBYAR TE 'CHI MED 'OD

SNANG GI RDUL TSON DKYIL 'KHOR LA BRTEN PA'I ZHABS BRTAN RGYAS
PA PHUL,

TSESo BCUo GSUMo SNGAo MARo CO NE BLO BZANG NYI MAS GOS LEGS PA
YUG BDUN CU, DKYUS MA YUG

SUM CU, DNGUL SRANG LNGA BRGYA, KHA BTAGS NYIN BDE MA BCU, CHE
BA LNGA BCU (33NA) BKRAS BTAGS STONG,

SMAN YUG BRGYA, JA KO KHRA BRGYA SOGS STONG 'BUL BTEG ,DE MJUG
TU MI BZANG CHOS RJE SOGS 'KHOR

BCAS KYIS RANG RANG GI 'BUL NOD RGYA CHER BTEG ,DE NAS SKU NANG
MTSAMS BDUN PHRAG GCIG GNANG

@042

BA TSESo BCU DGU LAo GROL TSUL DANG, 'DI NYIN NAS BZUNG ZHAG
BDUN GYI BAR 'BRI GUNG GTER SGROM

NAS CHAB TSAN BZHES PA'I BKA' DRIN BSKYANGS TSUL BYAS, TSESo
BCUo BDUNo LA BYANG STAG RTZE 'OL KHA

MTHONG SMON PA BSOD NAMS NOR BU SER DANG ZLOS PA'I BRJE TSAB
RGYAL RTZE SKYONG NGA BA TSE DBANG RDO RJE

RDZONG BDA' BYAS, NYERo GNYISo LAo RJEo BLAo MA'Io DGONGS RDZOGS
SU DMIGS, 'BRAS SPUNGS DGA' LDAN PHO

BRANG GI TSOMS CHEN PHYAM GLING BYANG MA'I GNAM RGYAN LA GAN GOS
GZHI DMAR RGYA YIG MA KHA BCU GCIG,

KHA THI GZHI DMAR KHA NYI SHU RTZA GNYIS DANG, GZHI SER KHA
PHYED BCU GSUM, GZHI SNGON KHA PHYED BCU DGU,

LHO RAS YUG BRGYAD, GZIMS CHUNG BKA' GDAMS YANG RTZE'I RTEN
KHRI'I DBU THOG GNAM RGYAN LA GOS

GZHI DMAR RGYA YIG MA KHA LNGA, KHA THI GZHI SER KHA'I SUM CHA
GNYIS, COD LDAN GZHI SNGON KHA PHYED GSUM,

RGYAB SHA LHO RAS YUG GCIG ,YANG GZIMS CHUNG BKA' GDAMS YANG
RTZE'I GNAM RGYAN LA GOS GZHI

DMAR RGYA YIG MA KHA PHYED GSUM, KHA THI GZHI SER KHA GANG, COD
LDAN SNGON PO KHA DO, RGYAB SHA RAS YUG

GCIG DANG KHA PHYED BZHI, BZO BO'I DO DAM BYA SGO BA BLO BZANG
DBANG PHYUG GIS BGYIS PA, GONG GSAL

GYI RI GONG (33BA) RNAMS BSDOMS PAR DNGUL SRANG BDUN CU DON
BRGYAD DANG ZHO BRGYAD SKAR PHYED GSUM

DRUG CHA GCIG BYUNG BA 'BRUR PHAB SRANG RER RU'I KHAL BCU GNYIS
RE RTZIS NAS KHAL DGU BRGYA ZHE LNGA BRE

BCO BRGYAD PHUL DO LHAG BCAS SONG,

TSESo NYERo GSUM LAo SDEo SRID ZUR BZHUGS GNYIS, RNAM RGYAL GRA
TSANG, GRONG SMAD BCAS NAS JA GSAR

PHUL, TSESo NYERo BRGYADo LAo RONG BYAMS CHEN GYI GRA PA NGAG
DBANG LEGS PAS BRGYAD STONG PA DANG MDO SDUD

PA'I RGYUGS PHUL, TSA BA MDZO SPOM DU BLA MAR BLO GLING DKA' BCU
BLO BZANG SNYING PO RDZONG BDA' BYAS, TSESo

GNAMo GANG LAo RVA SGRENG MKHAN PO DANG, DUR SBOD TSE DBANG GI
MI SNAR PHYAG MDUD, ,DAM RDZAS GNANG CHA

BCAS THON,

ZLA BA BCU PA'Io TSESo BCU GNYISo LAo RGYAL THANG RJONG SDOD
BRGYA RGAN PA TSE BRTAN RDO RJE RDZONG BDA' BYAS,

TSESo BCUo GSUMo LAo CHAR 'BABS PA SOGS LA KHAG BTAGS KYI DE
'PHRAL DGONGS RDZOGS SU KHAMS SU

@043

BKA' 'GYUR TSAR BCU GNYIS DANG, DVAGS GRA TSANG DU MA nI DUNG
PHYUR GCIG ,GZHAN YANG 'CHAR KA DANG

YANG GSANG GI GTOR BZLOG ,TSE SGRUB KHAG BZHI, RGYUD STOD SMAD
GNYIS KYI MGON CHOS DANG, BKRA SHIS

RTZER GUR ZHAL PU TRA'I BSKANG BA, 'KHOR LO 'BAR BA DRUG 'BUM,
DBUS GTZANG GI DGON AANG DANG LA

KHAL DO MA DANG AANG GNYIS LA PHYED DO MA'I RTZIS KYI MANG
'GYED, NGEDo KYIo RIM GROR GDUGS DKAR

'BUM THER, 'BUM BRGYA, GSER 'OD STONG PHRAG PHYED GNYIS, TSE
CHOG KHAG LNGA, TSES GZUNGS SA YA GCIG,

'KHOR LO 'BAR BA BZHI 'BUM (34NA) RNAMS, BSTANo SRIDo LAR RGYA'I
JUS RIM LA ZLA BA BCU PA'I

'CHAR CAN MA YIN PAR 'PHAR MA SER 'BRAS KYIS DBUS DGE DGON CHE
BA SUM CUS MDO SGRUB DANG

GTOR RGYAG ,DE PHYIN BDUN CUS SGROL MA, TSE PHUR GYI GTOR BZLOG
KHAG GSUM RNAMS, ZLAo BAo BCUo GCIGo

PA'Io TSESo GCIGo LAo RGYAL SRAS LHA BZANG KLU DBANG PO TA LAR
PHEBS PA'I 'BUL BA PHYAG MJAL BTEG,

DE NUB NAS BDUN GCIG GI BAR SKU MTSAMS BCAD RGYA GNANG KHUL
BYAS,

TSESo GNYISo LAo 'BRENG KHUD BLA MAR TSA SGO DBON PO RAB 'BYAMS
PA BLO BZANG DGE 'DUN DANG,

TSESo GSUMo LAo 'BRAS YUL SKYID TSAL GYI MKHAN POR NA LAndA ZUR
PA KUN NOR RDZONG BDA' BYAS, TSES

DRUGo LAo RNAM RGYAL GRA TSANG NAS NYI BZLOG SKU RIM AY'EE RING
CHIG 'BUM NYIS BRGYA DANG, TRIG KHROM CHIG

'BUM DRUG KHRI LNGA STONG, YANG TSESo BDUNo LAo GRA TSANG NAS
BSKANG GSO CHIG BRGYA NYER LNGA DANG GLUD RGYAS PA

SONG, TSESo BCU GNYISo LA RIN SPUNGS RDZONG SDOD 'DUS BYUNG SKYI
SPUG PA DANG GRA PHYI THANG KHROM DGOS DGOS

GNYIS RONG BYAMS CHEN PA DANG ZLOS PA SOGS KYI BRJE MAR GLANG BU
BSOD NAMS DPAL 'BAR DANG

'GOL MON NAM MKHA' GNYIS RDZONG BDA' BYAS,

TSESo BCOo LNGAo LA DGE SLONG NGAG DBANG DKON COG MA SPUN SRING
MO DANG BCAS PAS 'BUL YON SBYAR

BA'I RNAM RGYAL GRA TSANG NAS GZIMS CHUNG BRTAN BZHUGS SMIN
RGYAS SU PHUL, TSESo NYERo GNYISo LAo GRONG

SMAD GZHIS KA NAS NA BZA' SKOR CHA TSANG SOGS 'BUL BA DPANGS
MTHO BA DANG, RNAM (34BA) RGYAL GRA

TSANG DU SKU YON, DRUNG 'KHOR RNAMS LA STON MO DANG BCAS DVANGS
MA BCUD 'DREN LA BRTEN PA'I BRTAN

@044

BZHUGS BZABS PA PHUL, TSESo NYERo BDUN LAo DGA' LDAN PHUN TSOGS
GLING DU GSAR BRKOS RDO RJE BRAG

SPRUL SKUS MDZAD PA'I 'DUS PA MDO DBANG GI BLA BRGYUD KYI RNAM
THAR DANG, MDO DBANG GI CHOG BSGRIGS

BCAS PA 'BYOR, CHOS SKYONG GI GSUNG BA LTAR MYURo PHEBSo 'PHRIN
BCOL DU, SNGAGS KHANG, GNAS CHUNG

LCOG ,DPAL LHA LCOG ,DGA' LDAN MGON KHANG RNAMS SU BSKANG GSO
NYIN LNGA RE DANG, NGEDo CUNG ZHIG

KHAMS MA BDE BAR GTZUG LAG MO PHYVA BYAS PA BCAS RIM GROR BSKANG
BA NYIN GSUM RE, RGYAL DU LHA MOR

KHRI DANG CHOS SRUNG GZHAN RNAMS LA STONG RTZA, DGE DGON THAMS
CAD LA MGON CHOS KYI BSKANG BA JA SBYOR

SBREL RER GRA PA BCU RER BTANG, LHA SAR SGO MANG BLO GLING
BRGYAS BKA' 'GYUR TSAR GCIG ,GSER 'OD

LNGA BRGYA ZHE GSUM, THANG YIG BRGYA RTZA, BDE YANGS PA LNGA BCU
DANG, 'PHYONG RGYAS SU RI BO BDE CHEN DANG

BKRA SHIS BDE CHEN BSGRIL BA BRGYA, PHO BRANG DU RI BO CHOS
GLING PA DANG DAR RGYAS GLING PA BRGYA BCAS KYIS

SMAN BLA DANG MTSAN BRJOD, SER 'BRAS SU DKON BRTZEGS DANG BRGYAD
STONG PA BRGYA RTZA, JA TSUL BZHIR

GDUGS DKAR GANG 'GRO, SNGAGS PA LHUN GRUB CAN GYIS MA MO DGU
MDOS, SNGAGS KHANG, GNAS CHUNG,

DPAL LHA LCOG RNAMS SU BSKANG GSO NYIN GSUM RE, RDZONG MGO LNGAR
DGRA LHA DBANGS BSTOD NYIN GANG MA

RE, GTOR MA 'BUM THER (35NA) RNAMS, GLUD RDZONGS LE TSAN DANG,
BRGYAD STONG PA DANG GSER 'OD

BRGYA RTZA, LHA SAR DKON GNYER PAS GDUGS DKAR DANG BYANG CHUB
GLING PAS KHRO ROL, RGYAB CHOS BRAG

DBAR BAS GDUGS DKAR BRGYAD KHRI NYIS STONG DANG, DGE DGON SUM CU
SO GNYIS SU MANG JA GNYIS

RER GDUGS DKAR GANG THONGS, YANG KHAMS DBUS GRA TSANG KHAG BZHI
NAS SMAN BLA CHIG KHRI LNGA STONG,

THANG YIG CHIG STONG BZHI BRGYA, GDUGS DKAR 'BUM THER, LUG
BRGYA'I SROG BLU DANG, KLU 'BUM TSAR

MANG BA BCAS BTANG, TSESo NYERo DGUo LAo GTER STON RIN PO CHE
PHO BRANG CHEN POR PHEBS TE MJAL KHA

GNANG TSUL BSTAN, GNAMo GANGo LAo TSE DBANG RATNA'I RTA NAG GI
BKA' DBANG,

ZLAo BAo BCUo GNYISo PA'Io TSESo GCIGo LAo GDON 'GROL, RATNA'I
GUR DRAG RNAMS KYI BKA' DBANG

'BUL BZHES KYI TSUL, TSESo GNYISo LAo PAD RDOR CHOS MDZAD 'JAM
DBYANGS DBANG RGYAL PHA SPUN BCAS

@045

PAS 'BUL YON SBYAR BA'I RNAM RGYAL GRA TSANG NAS GZIMS CHUNG
BRTAN BZHUGS SMIN RGYAS SU PHUL, TSESo

LNGAo LAo GRA THANG GI MKHAN POR RNAM RGYAL GSER KHANG BLA MA
SANGS RGYAS BSTAN 'DZIN RDZONG BDA' BYAS,

TSESo BRGYADo LAo PHUR SGRUB 'CHAR CAN BZHIN TSUGS, KHAMS BYA MO
SNA DANG 'BROM THANG BLA MAR BE SER LHUN

GRUB RGYA MTSO RDZONG BDA' BYAS, TSESo BCUo LAo GTER STON RIN PO
CHE RJEo BLAo MA'Io ZHABS PHYIR NGED YOD TSUL

BYAS GDON 'GROL DANG BYAD 'GROL,

TSESo BCOo LNGAo LAo GZA'I DUG DBYUNG SROG DBANG GTOR DBANG DANG
BCAS PA 'BUL GNANG GI (35BA)

TSUL SNGAR BZHIN BYAS, CHOS SKYONG GI GSUNG DANG BCAS DGONGSo
RDZOGS MYUR PHEBS SKU RIM DU BDE

YANGS PAS PO TA LAR SMAN BLA LNGA STONG, SER 'BRAS BU ZHABS
BRTAN DANG GDUGS DKAR, DGA' LDAN

DU JA TSUL DANG, LHA SAR SGO MANG BLO GLING BSDO SAM PAS BRGYAD
STONG PA DGU BRGYA SO BDUN, GSER 'OD

STONG DANG NYIS BRGYA NYI SHU, GDUGS DKAR BDUN KHRI BDUN STONG,
LHA SA PO TA LAR RGYAGS BRDAN, KHRUS

GSOL, THAG NYE'I RDZONG GZHIS SUM CU SKOR LA DGRA LHA DBANGS
BSTOD, YUL GRU SO SOR SPYI RIM SNGON MA

RNAMS DANG MTSUNGS PA, BSTAN MA BCU GNYIS KYI GNAS SO SOR DAR
LCOG GSOL KHA BSANGS BCAS,

RGYUD STOD SMAD LA JA TSUL, SNGAGS KHANG DANG GNAS CHUNG LA
BZABS GSOL RNAMS DANG TSES NYERo GSUMo

LA TSE BDAG SGRUB MCHOD SNGAR RGYUN BZHIN DANG, GTER STON RIN PO
CHE DPON SLOB GRA BCAS KYIS BSTAN

MA LCOG TU GSHIN RJE'I GTOR BZLOG BDUN GCIG TSUGS, NYERo BRGYADo
LAo GUNG THANG GI SNYAN DAR KHA

BYANG, TSES GCIG GTOR CHEN DUS DPAL LDAN LHA MOR 'BUL RGYU'I
SNYAN DAR RNAMS KYI KHA BYANG BKA'

RTZOM DANG, NYER DGU'I GTOR RGYAG GZIGS MO'I TSUL SNGAR LTAR
BYA,

@046

RAB BYUNG BCU GCIG PA'I SHING BYI LO'I NANG RJE BLA MA'I DGONGS
RDZOGS SU

DMIGS TE 'DUS SDE KHAG NAS RIM GRO MDZAD SKOR SOGS,

MIGo DMARo ZHESo PAo SHINGo PHOo BYI BAo GNAMo LOo GSARo TSESo
KYI SRID GSUM BDAG MO DUS KYI MCHOD

PA SOGS SNGAR RGYUN LTAR DANG, RTEN 'DOGS KYI TSOGS 'KHOR GDAN
BZHES THOG NANG DU NGED DANG BSTAN

'DZIN D'A LAS RGYAL PO, SE CHEN DBON PO RNAMS SNGA MA BZHIN
DANG, HUNG THA'I JI DANG B'A DUR THA'I JI SOGS

KHAMS GSUM DU BZHUGS PA'I (36NA) GZHAN MA SNGA LO BZHIN, GUNG
TSIGS GRAL LA GTER STON RIN PO

CHE SKU ZHABS SU PHEBS KHUL GYI BDE BA CAN DU BZHUGS, TSOMS CHEN
DU NGED DANG RGYAL PO, D'A LAS HUNG

THA'I JI, BKRA SHIS B'A DUR THA'I JI, RNAM RGYAL SOGS BYANG RIGS
KYI RGYAL KHAG ,DPON CHUNG JA'I SANG

SOGS DANG, 'JAM DBYANGS GONG MA RGYAL PO'I MI SNA RGAN GZHON
'GRUL BSDEBS PA DANG BCAS PA,

CHOS SDE CHEN PO PHAN TSUN GYI BLA SLOB DPON, RGYUN GYI DRUNG
'KHOR, SDE SRID SNE'U SDONG RTZE DANG SA SKYA'I SKU TSAB

SOGS PHYOGS MTHA'I LO GSAR 'BUL MI RNAMS DANG BCAS DGA' STON
THOG GAR ROL GRAL 'PHROS

SOGS SNGAR RGYUN LTAR DANG, TSES GNYIS LA GRAL NYIN SNGA MA'I
RAG BSDUS STENG GRA TSANG PHAN BDE LEGS

BSHAD GLING PA YONGS RDZOGS, RIN CHEN RGYAN CHA BA LNGA BCU LHAG
BCAS, BKRA SHIS RDZAS RTAGS 'BUL

BA, MCHOD SPRIN SNA BRGYAD SOGS SNGAR RGYUN LTAR RGYAS PAR BYAS
SO,,

RAKshA KshIR SHO LO KA GNYIS KA BYA BA RANG BZHIN BRJOD PA, 'BOD
SUM LDAN SHING PHO BYI'I, ,GNAM LO'I DBANG

PHYUG GSAR DU LEGS BZHAD PA'I, MCHOD DANG DUS KYI DGA' STON
RLABS CHEN POR, ,BYANG PHYOGS NOR

'DZIN LA SPYOD MONG GOL DANG, ,'PHAGS YUL YA TSE NEE PA LA'I
LJONGS SU, ,STOBS KYI DPUNG LDAN SNA

TSOGS BYA MA RTA, ,GNYUG MAR GNAS SOGS SKYE 'GRO GRANGS MED
BCAS, ,GNA' BO'I LUGS BZANG

SHIS PA'I CHO GA BSTAR, ,ZHES BAR SKABS KYI TSIGS SU BCAD PA'O,,

@047

GTER STON RIN PO CHES ZHABS PHYIR NGED YOD KHUL SME BRTZEGS
(36BA) KYI SGONAS BYAB KHRUS

DANG, TSESo GSUMo LAo RTA MGRIN SKYER SGANG LUGS KYI DBANG BZHI
BYIN RLABS KYI TSUL DU 'BUL BA GNANG

TSUL BYAS, TSESo BDUNo LAo PHUN TSOGS GLING GNYER SDOD KHANG
GSER MA SHES RAB DPAL BZANG GI BRJE

MAR SHUN RGYA MA BA DGOS SKYES, 'DUL BA DANG SDING KHA'I BLA MA
RAB 'BYAMS PA DGA' LDAN GYI TSAB BDE

YANGS RAB 'BYAMS PA SLE MA BLO BZANG BSTAN 'DZIN RDZONG BDA'
BYAS, TSESo BRGYADo LAo DGONGS RDZOGS

RNAM DKAR DU 'OL KHA DKON GNYER BA DUNG PA GNYIS THE BA'I BCUS
LO GSAR TSES GCIG GTOR 'BUL

BYED PA'I MCHOD CHAS MKHAR RU'I BAR ZHIB KHAL GCIG ,MAR NYAG
BZHI, DMAR RGYAN CHUNG BRGYAD CU GRAS

GCIG ,MCHOD 'BRU PHUL BZHI, SNUM ZANGS MGO DO, GU GUL LCAGS MGO
GANG, SPOS RENG GSUM, DKAR

MO LAG G-YAS, MDA' DAR GCIG ,TSOGS SHA CHUNG BCU ZUG GCIG ,LAG
SDOGS BCU GCIG ,THUD

LEB BZHI, KHAM STAR 'DRES PA BRE GANG PHUL LNGA, PHYE MAR RTZAM
SHOR KHAL GCIG ,MAR NYAG DO, PHUD CHANG

TIG DO, JA THUG LTO YON BSDOMS PAR JA NYAG GANG, MAR NYAG DGU
SPOR DO, NAS BRE LNGA PHUL DO, RTZAM

KHAL GCIG BRE BCO BRGYAD PHUL DO, TSA PHUL GANG, PHYUR BA BRE
GSUM PHUL BZHI, SNUM PHUL PHYED BZHI,

CHUNG KHOG PHYED DANG DRUG ZUG GCIG BCAS 'BRUR PHAB RU'I KHAL
BCU BRE BDUN PHUL PHYED BZHI BCU CHA

GCIG ,RDZONG GI GTONG DEB NANG GSAL MCHOD YUL RNAMS KYI JA THOB
SNGA SOR (37NA) DKYUS JA 'U ZI

GTONG BA 'DI LO NAS BZUNG BZANG JAR GA BSGYUR BA'I DGA' ZHAN BAR
KHYAD 'BRUR PHAB RU'I KHAL NYIS

BRGYA DRUG BRE DO DANG, LO STAR RGYAL MTSAN DAR LCOG BRJE SKABS
DKON GNYER PA BRGYAD KYIS LHA BSANGS,

SHIS BRJOD BYED PA'I DGOS CHA MCHOD CHAS BSDOMS PA MKHAR RU'I
NAS BRE GSUM, RTZAM BRE BCU GSUM

RNAMS SBYOR 'JAGS BYAS,

TSESo DGU LAo RTA RA MDO PA BLO BZANG LHUN GRUB LA GSANG BRTOL
ZHING GAN RGYA BLANGS, HUNG THA'I JI MA

NAS PHEBS BZHED 'DUG PA DANG, 'GAGS CHE 'DI RIGS YON BDAG GNANG
CHE BAS ZHU BA SKABS SU

@048

BABS PA NGOS KYIS MA MJAL BAR THOG MA'I BSLAB STON GYI BABS DANG
DBU RTZI SOGS NAS MA THUB PA

DGONGS SBYAR GYI PHEBS TSUL ZHUS PA LO SNGON MA'I ZLA BA BCU
GCIG PA'I TSES LNGA LA LHA SAR PHEBS KYANG

SKU NA MTHO BA DANG SNYUNG GZHI 'DRA BCAS RIM GYIS TSES BRGYAD
BAR GSANG BRTOL MA THUB CING DE NYIN

RAGS TZAM DANG, TSESo BCU'Io NYINo HUNG THA'I JI DANG, BKRA SHIS
B'A DUR THA'I JI, AER TE NI B'A DUR,

RGYAL PO'I SRAS LHA BZANG KLU DBANG, GAD PO KHANG GSAR BA RNAMS
KYI PHYAG THAM DANG THE'U SOGS BLANGS,

HUNG THA'I JI DANG AER TE NA B'A DUR LA THUGS DOGS MANG BA DANG,
RVA SGRENG MDOR PHEBS DGONGS RJEo BLAo

MAo SRIDo ZHI'Io GTZUGo RGYANo NYID SKU NA CHUNG CHUNG ZHIG
BYUNG BA NYE 'KHOR LA BSHAD TSUL GSUNG BA BLA MAR

THUGS DAD BRTAN GSHIS YIN 'DRA SNYAM, GZA' TSES PHUN SUM (37BA)
TSOGS PA DANG BCAS 'DI NYIN

CHOS SKYONG CHEN POS NGO BO RNAM GRANGS GSAL LA 'KHROL BA GNANG
TSUL LTAR SKU MTSAMS 'KHROL TZAM

GNANG BA'I 'JAM DBYANGS GONG MA RGYAL PO'I GSER YIG PA RGAN
GZHON GYIS GONG GI BKA' SHOG PHUL

ZHING, MI SNA NGO BO GNYIS 'GRUL SDEBS DANG BCAS KYI PHYAG MJAL
'BUL BA RGYAS PAR BTEG ,DE THOG

TU D'A LAS HUNG THA'I JI, BKRA SHIS B'A DUR THA'I JI, RNAM
RGYAL, AER TE NA B'A DUR, AER GE D'A'I CHING,

MER RGAN THA'I JI'I SRAS RAB BRTAN, AER KHE JO NONG, BSOD NAMS
DAR RGYAS, GU JA'I KHA'I RAB

BRTAN, AE BE LAS, CO NE CHOS RJE, DPON PO BLA, DBO CHUNG, RGYA
NAG 'GRUL SDEBS PA MNGA' RIS

RAB 'BYAMS PA, B'A RING GUN CHI'I MI SNA SKYA SER BZHI, AER KHE
WANG GI MI SNA RNAMS LA PHYAG DBANG JA

GRAL GNANG TSUL, DPON CHUNG GI GRAS THU MED AO CHIR THA'I JI YAB
SRAS GSUM, KHE CHIG ,KHOD CHA GAN,

BSTAN 'DZIN, MONG JA RAG GI RAB BRTAN, DBON CHUNG, BKRA SHIS,
AAG ,MKHA' 'GRO'I SRAS NE KHAL

THU, G-YON RU'I MI SNA BSTAN PA SHES RAB, PHUN TSOGS BKRA SHIS
KYI MI SNA, HUNG THA'I JI'I DRUNG YIG,

SMAN PA LNGA DAR, NA BZA' KHYER MI, B'A DUR THA'I JI'I JA SANG
MTSO KHAR LOG 'GRO MI, AU KHE RA DHAS B'A

DUR THA'I JI'I SRAS RAB 'BYAMS PA PHUN TSOGS BKRA SHIS, RVA
SGRENG MKHAN PO'I SHOG DGE SLONG STOD

DMAG NAS YONGS PA'I AER TE NA JU RIG TU, GU JA'I KHA'I MOO JA
RAG DGE TSUL MA, CHOS BZANG THA'I JI,

@049

BSOD NAMS DAR RGYAS, BSOD NAMS HUNG THA'I JI GSUM GYI DPON MO,
(28NA) KHOD RNAM RGYAL GYI YUM,

THOR KHOD CHOS SGROL MA, RAB BRTAN DANG DPON CHUNG GI DPON MO,
KHE CHIG THA'I JI'I SRAS MO, AAG GI MA,

AER KHE JO NONG GI AA LCE, RGYA NAG GI 'GRUL SDEBS AA PA KHA
DKON COG DANG, SPAS SE'I AER TE NA

DKA' BCU, 'OR DU SU GU RU SKYABS, DPAL LI'I BI MA LA THA'I THA'I
JI'I DKA' BCU SHES RAB YON TAN, THU

MED CHOS SKYABS THA YANG CHI'I BLO GROS DGE SLONG DANG, SO CHUG
DU DGE SLONG, HAR GDONG NGAG DBANG SBYIN

PA DGE SLONG, RGYA MTSO DGE TSUL, BAN SER NGAG DBANG RGYAL
MTSAN, 'OR DU SU GU RU SKYABS DPAL LI'I

DGONGSo RDZOGSo SU DMIGS SKU MCHOD DU DMAR LCAGS RA MO CHE LHA

PA BKRA SHIS KYI TSAB SHAR PA CHOS RJE CO NE TSUL KHRIMS DAR

DKAR DGONGS RDZOGS SU, BON LUNG PADMA CHOS GLING PAR KHAMS LUNG

GU RU'I SGRUB MCHOD DGOS CHA BZANG 'BRU KHAL SUM CU SO DRUG DANG

THAR PA CHEN PO, RJE BTZUN MI LA'I ZHABS RJES, RDO RJE GDAN GYI

MO SNGAR RGYUN BZHIN TSUGS,

STONG SKUD DMAR PO'I 'PHAR PHYIN GYI KA THO MTSAN BYANG YOD PA'I

BCU BZHI, PAGS BSE CHE CHUNG RGYA SAG TZAM

@081

BRGYAD RNAMS KYI RI GONG DNGUL SRANG BZHI STONG DGU BRGYA BZHI
BCU ZHE BDUN SKAR BRGYAD LHAG BCAS

RNAMS LAS BSKRUN PA'I DO DAM SNYE DGON RDO RJE RGYAL MTSAN DANG,
GZHON BDE GROG MKHAR BA LHA MGON,

SHOG LAS PA NYI SHU (62NA) BCAS PAS LAS RGYUN ZLA BA BDUN DANG,
LTO GAR BA BZHI, ZHUS DAG PA DRUG,

BRIS DMANGS BZO PHRAN LAS BYED BCAS BYINGS MI GRANGS BRGYA PHRAG
GCIG DANG LNGA BCU NGA LNGA SKOR GYIS

ZLA BA LNGA DANG ZHAG DRUG ,GLEGS SHING BZO RTZI'I DO DAM 'BOG
GONG BLO GROS RGYAL MTSAN, RKANG MA LHA RTZE

LHUG PA BLO BZANG SHES RAB, SHING BZO BA LHA SA BLO BZANG CAN
BCU DRUG ,DNGUL BRIS PA SKYA KHA SANGS

RGYAS CAN BCU BDUN, DNGUL 'DUL 'BA' LHUG CAN BCU GNYIS RNAMS
KYIS BGYIS PA NAS BZAD

GZHIS KAR GTOGS PA GANG YIN LA PHOGS DGOS CHA SPROD MI GZHIS
SDOD CHU MIG KHA PA LNGA 'DZOM, DE

'PHROS LA DAR RGAN DKA' BCUS BYAS PA'I GONG GSAL SKU RGYU PHOGS
STON YON SOGS KHYON SHOR KHAL

BRGYAD KHRI BRGYAD STONG DGU BRGYA SO BZHI BRE GANG PHUL GANG
LHAG BCAS RNAMS LAS BSGRUBS PA LO KHOGS

'DI NANG DU DBU BTZUGS PA GRUB PAR NYE BA'I DKAR CHAG ,MCHOD
SPRIN SNA BRGYAD KYI DEB KYI 'GO BRJOD

RNAMS BKA' RTZOM TSUL DU SONG,

GNAMo GANGo LAo 'PHAN YUL GSAS KHANG BLA MA GRA BCAS KYIS 'BUL
BA SNGON DU 'GRO BA'I BRTAN

BZHUGS PHUL, TSER GSEB CHOS SKYONG GIS BRTAN BZHUGS TSIGS BCAD
'DI BZHIN RTEN 'BREL KHYAD

NAS DGON KHA SHAS LA 'DZUGS DGOS TSUL SER 'BRAS DGE GSUM GYI
DBUS SKYID SHOD DBUR STOD

BCAS PA'I DGON PA BRGYAR MANG JA SBYOR 'BREL DANG BCAS ZLA STOD
NAS BTZUGS, HUNG THA'I HIR MJAL

KHA GNANG BA'I RKYEN SEL DU CHOS SKYONG CHEN POS BSLAB STON
GNANG TSUL GYI DON MYUR PHEBS SU DMIGS

SER (62BA) 'BRAS GNYIS SU JA TSUL BCU BZHI RE DANG, DGA' LDAN DU
BRGYAD BCAS PAR SHER SNYING

'GRO GANG CHE, YER PAR GRA SLOB BRGYA DANG NYER DGUS GSER 'OD
TSAR STONG DANG BDUN, 'PHAGS PA'I SKU

MDUN DU BDE YANGS PA BRGYAS SA GSUM MA CHIG KHRI NYIS STONG DANG
SMAN BLA CHIG STONG BZHI BRGYA, GDUGS

DKAR LNGA BRGYA, SHER SNYING SUM STONG LNGA BRGYA, MCHOD 'BUL
GANG RGYAS DANG BCAS PA, LHA SAR DGA'

@082

LDAN PHUN TSOGS GLING GRA SLOB BRGYA DANG GSUM GYIS GDUGS DKAR
BZHI KHRI DRUG STONG BRGYAD BRGYA DRUG CU

RE LNGA DANG, 'PHAN YUL GSAS KHANG PA GRA PA DGU BCU GO DRUG
,THANG SKYA BA GRA PA DRUG CU RE BRGYAD, STAR

PHU BA GRA PA DRUG CU BCAS PAS GSER 'OD BZHI STONG LNGA BRGYA
LNGA BCU NGA BDUN, SHER SNYING NYIS 'BUM

NYIS STONG CHIG BRGYA DRUG CU, TSE GZUNGS SUM KHRI BZHI STONG,
GDUGS DKAR DRUGU BRGYA BRGYAD CU, SGROL

MA CHIG 'BUN DRUG KHRI BDUN STONG DRUG BRGYA BRGYAD CU, PHYI
NANG GI THAN LTAS NGAN PA BZLOG THABS SU MO

PHY'A BGYIS PA'I GZHIS RTZE SOGS RDZONG 'GO LNGAR DGE DGON 'BREL
CHAGS NAS GRA PA BRGYA RES ZLA GCIG

RING GDUGS DKAR GANG 'GRO, RIN SPUNGS SOGS RDZONG GZHIS BDUN DU
RNYING DGON 'BREL MTSUNGS

NAS SGRUB ZHAG BDUN SNGON DU 'GRO BA'I KHRO ROL GYI GTOR BZLOG
,RGYAB CHOS PA DGE DGON TSO BSDUS

BRGYA RE ZHAG GONG MTSUNGS SHER SNYING GANG 'GRO, SER 'BRAS DGE
GSUM LA JA TSUL BCO LNGAR SHER SNYING

NYIS 'BUM DRUG KHRI BRGYAD STONG, RDO RJE BRAG DANG SMIN GROL
GLING DU MANG JA LNGA BCU YON (63NA) BCAS SO

SOR 'KHOR LO 'BAR BA SA YA GNYIS DANG SUM 'BUM BRGYAD KHRI NYIS
STONG SUM BRGYA NYER LNGA, GONG DKAR

DU RDO RJE BRAG PAS 'CHAR KA'I GTOR BZLOG,

RJEo BLAo MA SRID ZHI'Io GTZUGo RGYAN MCHOG GI DGONGS RDZOGS SU
'PHYONG RGYAS RI BO BDE CHEN PAS

MTSAN BRJOD CHIG 'BUM NYIS STONG, PO TA LAR BDE YANGS PAS SPYAN
'DREN KHRUS GSOL CHIG STONG LNGA

BRGYA, LTUNG BSHAGS CHIG 'BUM BRGYAD KHRI, GZHIS RTZER NGOR PA
BRGYAS ZLA GCIG BAR RNAM 'JOMS GANG

'GRO, 'DUS BYUNG DU DBANG LDAN CHOS 'KHOR BA DANG, GSER SDINGS
PA BSGRIL BAS BZANG SPYOD CHIG

'BUM LNGA STONG NYIS BRGYA, 'DA' KA YE SHES CHIG 'BUM NYIS KHRI,
MTSO SNAR CHOS SDE BAS SHER SNYING SUM

F'BUM CHIG KHRI LNGA STONG DGU BRGYA, LTUNG BSHUGS NYIS 'BUM
BDUN KHRI STONG LNGA BRGYA, LHA RTZER 'OG MIN

GLING PAS RDO RJE SDER MO TSAR BZHI KHRI LNGA BRGYA, GDUGS DKAR
LNGA KHRI DGU STONG DGU BRGYA BZHI BCU, NGED

RANGo GI RIM GROR PHO BRANG DU RI BO CHOS GLING PA DANG DAR
RGYAS GLING PA BSGRIL BAS MTSAN BRJOD TSAR CHIG

'BUM SUM KHRI LNGA STONG CHIG BRGYA, SGROL MA CHIG KHRI BRGYAD
BRGYA BZHI BCU, TSE GZUNGS DRUG KHRI BZHI STONG

@083

DRUG CU, SGROL DKAR GYI GZUNGS BDUN KHRI BZHI STONG DRUG CU,
SHER SNYING DRUG STONG SUM BRGYA DON GNYIS,

RTZE LHA SGANG DU CHAB NAG PA DANG BKRA SHIS RAB BRTAN PA BSGRIL
BAS GTZUG TOR DKAR NAG GANG 'GRO,

RGYAL RTZER DPAL 'KHOR CHOS SDE NAS DGE DGON TSO BSDUS KYI GDUGS
DKAR MCHOG GRUB BRGYAD KHRI

BDUN BRGYA BCU DGU, GTZUG TOR 'BAR MA NYIS (63BA) 'BUM BDUN KHRI
LNGA STONG BZHI BRGYA DON GNYIS,

LUS NGAG YID GSUM BCINGS PA LAS GROL BA NYIS 'BUM NYIS KHRI DGU
STONG CHIG BRGYA RE GSUM, SDONG

RGYAN NYIS KHRI DGU STONG CHIG BRGYA RE BDUN, PHYIR BZLOG RNAM
RGYAL NYIS 'BUM BDUN KHRI BZHI STONG SUM

BRGYA RE GSUM, PA SNAM DU MTSAN SGROG PAS GDUGS DKAR CHIG 'BUM
CHIG KHRI DGU STONG BRGYAD BRGYA

BRGYAD CU RNAMS SONG, LONG PO BKRA SHIS CHOS GLING DU BDE YANGS
RAB 'BYAMS PA NGAG DBANG BSAM

GTAN, RNGOD RGYA MTSO GLING DANG AA RIG THANG BLA MAR BDE YANGS
DKA' BCU NGAG DBANG SMON LAM GNYIS RDZONG BDA' BYAS,

ZLAo BAo BRGYAD PA'Io TSESo GCIGo LAo RDZONG SDOD SBYOR RA BAS
'GO BYAS RGYAL RTZE RDZONG 'OG DPAL 'KHOR

CHOS SDE DANG BCAS PA'I LHA SDE MI SDE TSANG MAS 'BUL YON TSOGS
'KHOR DPANGS MTHO BA SBYAR TE RNAM

RGYAL GRA TSANG NAS 'CHI MED 'OD SNANG LA BRTEN PA'I ZHABS BRTAN
RGYAS PA PHUL, TSESo GNYISo NASo DRANG

SRONG DBANG PO Ri shIS DUG SBYANGS PA'I YAN LAG BRGYAD LDAN GYI
KHRUS CHOG NYIN BDUN GYI BAR 'PHAGS

PA'I SKU MDUN DU BSTEN PA GNANG BA'I TSUL BGYIS, TSESo BZHIo LAo
SHU STAG STAG RTZE DGON GYI KHA 'DZIN

'BRUG LA BLA MA 'OR PA CHOS MDZAD KYI NYIS LCOGS KYI BKOD PA
DANG, GANGS CAN CHOS 'PHEL DU STOD

ZUR PA SPO BO RAB 'BYAMS PA BLO BZANG RGYAL MTSAN DANG TSES BDUN
LAo GNYA' NANG 'PHEL GLING DU RME RU

BA BSOD NAMS RGYAL MTSAN BCAS RDZONG BDA' BYASo TSES BCUo NASo
BCU DRUG BAR NYIN STAR GYI 'JA'

SPRIN DANG, 'DI NYIN KHANG SER MA'I THAD NAS PO TA LAR 'JA' GUR
KHYAD MTSAR BA'ANG BYUNG (64NA)

'DUG ,TSESo BCU GCIGo NAS 'PHAGS PA LHA KHANG GI SKU MDUN DU
GZIMS GUR GNANG BA'I RDO RJE GRO LOD

KYI SKU MTSAMS BDUN PHRAG GCIG GNANG TSUL BGYIS SHING,

@084

TSESo BCOo LNGAo LAo THON PA NANG MTSAMS KHRUN GCOD KYI BGOD
PHUD GRAS SNE MO GZHIS KA NAS PHYIR

'GRO DGOS PA DA CHA GZHUNG 'DZIN GYI 'DZIN BDAG 'PHOS PA'I MI
'JAGS GRAS RNAM DKAR DGONGS

RDZOGS SU DMIGS, BU LUGS RU DGON PAR DUS 'KHOR SGRUB MCHOD,
BTZAN KHANG RTZVE'I GTOR GZHI, NYA

NYI SHU MCHOD PA, RU TSO KHA BA'I DUS CHEN, GSHED DMAR SGRUB
MCHOD, BTZAN KHANG RTZVE'I GTOR GZHI, NYA

STONG DGU GTOR, CHOS KHRIMS PA'I PHOGS BCAS PA'I LO 'KHOR GYI
DGOS CHA BSDOMS BZANG 'BRU RU'I

KHAL SUM BRGYA DANG BZHI BRE BRGYAD PHUL LNGA BCU CHA PHYED
GNYIS, BRA'O KHAL GSUM, TSVA BRE BCU GNYIS

PHUL PHYED DO DRUG CHA GCIG ,SNUM KHAL GCIG BRE DGU, YAGS JU
NYAG DO SPOR GANG BCU CHA PHYED GNYIS,

SHA SHAN DANG 'U ZI PHYED 'DRES KHAL GNYIS NYAG BCU GCIG ,MAR
KHAL DGU NYAG DGU SPOR GSUM BZHI

CHA GCIG ,CHUNG SHA BZHI GLING GCIG DANG BCU GZUGS PHYED GNYIS,
KLUNGS TSAG BUGS 'BRING PHYED BZHI

DANG BCU GZUGS PHYED GNYIS, LUG MGO BDUN, NYA LEB BCU DRUG ,LAG
SDOGS BCU DRUG ,SMAN BAR

KHA GANG, DAR KHA LNGA, LHO RAS KHA BZHI, KLUNG KO'I BZHI CHA
GCIG BCAS 'BRUR PHAB RU'I KHAL SUM BRGYA

BRGYAD CU GYA GSUM BRE BZHI PHUL PHYED LHAG BCAS RNAMS, RTZE
TSOGS PAR PHOGS THEBS LO (64BA)

GCIG GI THOB RNAMS BSDOMS 'BRU RU'I KHAL BDUN BRE BCU GCIG PHUL
DO, RTZAM BRE LNGA, BKRAS BTAGS

GCIG ,DKYUS BTAGS GCIG ,SMAN RNYING KHA GANG, SMAN GSAR KHA DO,
SPEN 'DAB CHE TSAD GCIG ,LHO

RAS KHA GSUM, LUG SHA LAG PA PHYED, LTO LNGA SDER GNYIS, RKYANG
SDER SPEL MA GSUM BCAS 'BRUR PHAB

MKHAR KHAL BCU DRUG BRE DGU PHUL DO LHAG BCAS RNAMS RGYUN 'JAGS
BYAS, TSESo BCU DRUGo LAo KHYAD PAR

NUB PHYOGS NAS 'JA' G-YUNG DRUNG RIS DANG,

TSESo BCOo BRGYADo LA'ANGo NUB PHYOGS SU 'JA' SHIN TU GSAL BA
BYUNG, TSESo BCUo DGUo LAo GZIMS

CHUNG KHAMS GSUM DU PHEBS TSUL BGYIS, SHES DKAR CHOS SDE'I GRA
PA GSUNG RAB BSTAN 'DZIN GYIS

MNGON RTOGS RGYAN, DBU MA RTZA 'JUG GZHI GSUM, BLA MA LNGA BCU
PA, 'DUL BA RGYA MTSO'I SNYING PO RNAMS

RGYUGS PHUL, RNAM RGYAL GRA TSANG NAS NYIN LNGA'I BAR MYUR PHEBS
'PHRIN BCOL SPYI BSKANG DANG, BYAD SOGS

@085

LA DMIGS YANG BZLOG RDO RJE PHA LAM BYE BA GCIG DANG 'BUM TSO
GSUM SONG BA TSES BCU DRUG LA GROL

ZHING, TSESo BCUo BDUNo NAS GNAM GANG GI BAR AY'EE RING TSUGS
PAR BYE BA GCIG DANG NYIS KHRI SUM STONG

DGU BRGYA, TRIG KHROM MA BYE BA GCIG RNAMS SONG, TSESo NYIo SHU
LAo GDAN SA CHEN PO 'BROG DGA' LDAN

RNAM PAR RGYAL BA'I GLING NAS KHRI RIN PO CHE DANG ZUR PA RNAM
DAG RDO RJE'I SKU TSAB, RTZE SHAR CHOS RJE GNYIS,

THOS BSAM GLING DANG NYANG RONG GRA TSANG SLOB DPON, MNGON DGA'
SKU SKYE SOGS BLA SPYI GRA DMANGS DANG

BCAS (65NA) PA DANG, DE MTSAMS STAR BU BLA SPYI GRA DMANGS, LHA
LDAN RU BZHI SPYI TSOGS BSNYEN GNAS

MA DANG BCAS PAS RANG RANG GI 'BUL BA DANG MAndAL SNGON 'GRO'I
ZHABS BRTAN PHUL NYIo SHUo GNYISo SNGONo

MARo SPYI LUNG GI CHOS SDE BCU GSUM BCA' BA'I GRAS KAR LUGS
GSUNG RAB GLING PA'I SHUL DU SHING BYA RJEo

BLAo MA'Io BKA' LTAR MI DBANG BSOD NAMS RAB BRTAN GYIS RNYING
PA'I SON SOGS MED PAR BTZUGS

PA'I SHANGSo DGA'o LDANo CHOSo 'KHORo BLA SPYI THUN MONG NAS
'BUL YON SBYAR BA'I RNAM RGYAL GRA TSANG NAS

GZIMS CHUNG BRTAN BZHUGS DANG, DE MTSAMS CHOS KYI RGYAL PO SRONG
BTZAN SGAM PO'I DUS BRTZIGS

PAR KLU MES KYI ZHIG GSOS MDZAD DGE 'DUN GYI SDE BTZUGS JO NANG
LUGS SU YOD PA LAS SEMS

DPA' CHEN POS DGE LUGS SU BSGYUR BA THANGo SKYA BAo BLA MA GRA
BCAS KYIS 'BUL BA SNGON DU 'GRO BA'I

BRTAN BZHUGS PHUL, TSESo NYIo SHUo GNYISo PHYI MAR 'DUS BYUNG
KHUL DRAG BTZAN DANG BCAS PAS 'BUL

YON SBYAR BA'I RNAM RGYAL GRA TSANG NAS GZIMS CHUNG BRTAN BZHUGS
PHUL, STAR SDONG BLO BZANG TSE BRTAN

SPUN BU BCAS KYIS BKA' 'GYUR RIN PO CHE GSAR BZHENGS KYI DKAR
CHAG BKA' RTZOM TSUL DU SONG,

TSESo NYERo BDUN NAS CHOS RJE KHA RAG NAS KYIS RDO RJE SLOB DPON
BGYIS PA'I LHA SAR NGED KYI BYAD

BZLOG TU DMIGS YANG BZLOG GI SKU RIM TSUGS, ZLAo BAo DGUo PA'Io
TSESo GSUMo LAo GTING SKYES BKRA

SHIS CHOS GLING BLA MAR SGO MANG KHAR KHA BSTAN PA DAR RGYAS,
SHEL DKAR CHOS SDER BLO GLING RAB 'BYAMS

PA MI NYAG YE SHES RGYA MTSO, TSESo LNGAo LAo THANG SKYAR (65BA)
STOD BLA MA NGAG DBANG NAM MKHA' DANG, DGA'

LDAN CHOS GLING DU BYAMS GLING BLA ZUR RAB 'BYAMS PA DGA' LDAN
RNAMS RDZONG BDA' BYAS, TSESo BDUN

@086

LAo SGYID THANG NOR BUS 'BUL YON SBYAR BA'I RNAM RGYAL GRA TSANG
NAS GZIMS CHUNG BRTAN BZHUGS DANG,

DE MTSAMS DGA' LDAN DON GNYIS GLING PA BLA MA GRA BCAS KYI 'BUL
BA SNGON DU 'GRO BA'I BRTAN

BZHUGS, TSESo BRGYADo LAo NYE SKOR DRUNG 'KHOR DRAG ZHAN MI SER
SPYI BSDUS KYIS 'BUL YON SBYAR BA'I RNAM

RGYAL GRA TSANG NAS GZIMS CHUNG BRTAN BZHUGS, DE MTSAMS RJE SMON
LAM DPAL BAS BTAB CING DON

DPAL BAS KYANG DAR RGYAS SU BYAS PA 'PHYOSo BKRAo SHISo BDEo
CHENo BLA MA GRA DMANGS PHYED NYIS BRGYA SKOR

GYIS ZHABS BRTAN, DE 'THUD SEMS DPA' CHEN PO KUN DGA' BZANG POS
YAR GONG GNYIS LA SBYIN

BDAG BSKUL NAS ME RTA LOR BTAB PA'I ZUNGo MKHARo MDOo SNGAGSo
GLINGo BLA GRAS KYANG BRTAN BZHUGS

PHUL ZHING BLA MA KHA RU CHOS MDZAD NGAG DBANG RAB BRTAN GYIS
RGYUD BLA SOGS KYI LUNG DANG BCAS MGRIN

BA'I SGO BRGYA YANGS PAR PHYE,

TSESo BCUo LAo CHOS SDE BCU GSUM BCA' BA'I GRAS KAR LUGS BRGYAD
GRA'I SHUL DU SA BYI RJEo BLAo

MASo SA SKYONG BSOD NAMS RAB BRTAN DU BKA'I GNANG BA BSTZAL TE
RNYING PA'I GRA SON SOGS MED PAR

BTZUGS PA DOLo DGA'o LDANo GSUNGo RABo GLINGo BLA MA GRA DMANGS
NYIS BRGYA DRUG CUS 'BUL BA SNGON DU

'GRO BA'I BRTAN BZHUGS RNAMS PHUL, TSESo BCUo BDUNo LAo NGED LA
TSE RTA ZUNG 'BREL GYI BKA' DBANG

GNANG BA DANG, TSESo BCOo BRGYADo NASo ZHAG BDUN GYI BAR 'BRI
GUNG GTER SGROM NAS BZHES PA'I CHAB

TSAN BSTEN (66NA) PA GNANG TSUL BGYIS, DGA' LDAN GSUNG RAB GLING
GI GRA PA DKA' BCU GRAGS PA

PHUN TSOGS KYIS MDZOD RTZA 'GREL, 'JAM DBYANGS RGYA MTSOS PHAR
PHYIN GYI SPYI DON MTHA' GCOD, BLO

BZANG BSTAN PA, CHOS RGYA MTSO, NGAG DBANG BLO GROS GSUM GYIS
'GREL PA DON GSAL, MNGON RTOGS

RGYAN, DBU MA 'JUG PA, MDZOD KYI RTZA BA, 'DUL BA RGYA MTSO'I
SNYING PO RNAMS DANG, 'PHRIN LAS RGYA MTSOS

MNGON RTOGS RGYAN, DBU MA 'JUG PA, MDZOD RTZA, 'DUL BA RGYA
MTSO'I SNYING PO RNAMS KYI RGYUGS PHUL,

RNAM RGYAL GRA TSANG GI GRA PA NGAG DBANG NAM MKHAS DGE BSKOS
KYI 'JOG TU SRANG BCU BZHI LAS GRUB PA'I

DNGUL GYI PAD SDER PHUL BA'I KHA BYANG BKA' RTZOM TSUL DU SONG,
CHOS SKYONG CHEN PO'I GSUNG BZHIN RJEo BLAo

@087

MAo SRIDo ZHI'Io GTZUGo RGYANo MCHOGo GI DGONGS RDZOGS SU RANG
BYON LNGA LDAN GYI DRUNG DU BDE YANGS PAS SPYAN

'DREN KHRUS GSOL GANG RGYAS DANG, SMAN BLA CHIG STONG DRUG
BRGYA, SHEL DKAR CHOS SDE BAS YIG DRUG BYE

BA GNYIS DANG SA YA LNGA, DMIGS BRTZE MA LNGA 'BUM, PO TA LAR
RNAM RGYAL GRA TSANG DANG, LHA SAR SNGAGS

PA TSOS BSANGS BRNGAN GANG RGYAS, DGA' LDAN DON GNYIS GLING PA
DANG BKRA SHIS BDE CHEN PAS GDUGS

DKAR BRGYAD KHRI, TSES BRGYAD BCO LNGAR PO TA LAR 'JA' KHYIM NYI
ZLA G-YUNG DRUNG RIS SOGS DANG, ZLA BA

BRGYAD PA'I TSES NYER GSUM GYI NYIN PHYED YOL SA G-YOS SHIN TU
CHE BA LNGA TZAM DANG, ZLA BA DGU PA'I

TSES GNYIS KYI SROD LA CHE BA GNYIS DANG CHUNG BA GCIG (66BA) ME
TOG GI CHAR BYUNG BA BCAS PAR GARGA

DANG STAG RNA SOGS KYI LTAS KYI GTZUG LAG RNAMS LA HA CANG MI
LOD CING, CHE BA BYUNG DUS THUR SHING

BTZUGS PA'I MO PHYVA'I BSHAD PAR YANG MYUR PHEBS DANG NGED RANG
BCAS LA NGAN PA MA SHAR ZHING BSTAN

SRID LA YANG PHUGS LAS 'PHRAL MI NGAN YANG SKU RIM ZHABS BSKUL
ZHU MI MANG BA BCAS, RJEo BLAo MAo SRIDo

ZHI'Io GTZUGo RGYANo MCHOGo GI DGONGS RDZOGS SU GZHIS RTZE PHO
BRANG SOGS RDZONG 'GO BRGYAD DU SO SOR DGE

DGON 'BREL MTSUNGS NAS GRA PA BRGYAS ZLA GCIG RE SONG BAR BKA'
'GYUR TSAR LNGA BCU NGA BZHI, YUM

RGYAS 'BRING BSDUS GSUM TSAR RE, GZUNGS BSDUS TSAR CHIG STONG
LNGA BRGYA, PHAL CHEN CHIG KHRI LNGA BRGYA,

SA'I SNYING PO 'KHOR LO BCU PA'I MDO DGU 'BUM CHIG STONG NYIS
BRGYA, GDUGS DKAR CHIG 'BUM DRUG

STONG, SGROL MA NYIS KHRI DRUG STONG, SENG GDONG MA'I SNGAGS SUM
'BUM, TSE GZUNGS CHIG 'BUM LNGA STONG,

SHER SNYING BZHI KHRI LNGA STONG, LHA SA, BSAM YAS, KHRA 'BRUG
GSUM LA GSER CHAB DANG DKAR ME, MCHOD

PA BRGYA TSAR, MCHOD 'BUL DANG, SMAN BLA BRGYA GO BZHI, DE PHYIN
GNAS CHEN KHAG BZHI BCU ZHE DRUG LA

MCHOD PA BRGYA TSAR DANG DAR LCOG ,MCHOD 'BUL BA GRA PA BRGYA
RES SMAN BLA, BZANG SPYOD, BSAM PA LHUN

GRUB MA RNAMS 'GRO GANG CHE, PHA BONG KHA PAS LAN CHAGS GTOR MA
'BUM THER LHAG BCAS, KLU SBUG DANG

RA MO CHER GRA PA BZHI RES ZLA GCIG RING KLU GTOR GANG 'GRO,
CHOS 'KHOR RGYAL BAS RIL SGRUB DANG

'BREL BA'I (67NA) YIG DRUG DUNG PHYUR, PHO BRANG DU DAR GLING PA
DANG RI BO CHOS GLING BSDOMS PA, 'PHYONG

@088

RGYAS SU RI BO BDE CHEN PA, DGA' LDAN PHUN TSOGS GLING DU RANG
GRA BCAS PAS SMAN BLA DANG MTSAN BRJOD

'BUM THER RE, LHA SA BSAM YAS SOGS GNAS CHEN BCO LNGA SO SOR
NYIN GSUM GYI RING BLA MA'I LAS

BYANG DANG 'BREL BA'I BSAM PA LHUN GRUB MA DANG, TSOGS BRGYA,
BZHAD RI BO GRU 'DZIN DU YIG DRUG DUNG

PHYUR, GZHIS RTZER ZHA LU BAS GDUGS DKAR MDOS CHEN, SOG DGA'
LDAN RNAM GSUM DU GDUGS

DKAR 'BUM THER, MNGA' RIS KHYUNG RDZONG DU 'PHEL GLING PA DANG,
LHUN GRUB RDZONG DU RIN CHEN BRAG PA DANG

LHA KHANG PA BSGRIL BA BRGYA RES BKA' 'GYUR TSAR NYI SHU RTZA
LNGA, GSANG SNGAGS CHOS RDZONG DANG SHO MDOR GRA

PA BRGYA RES SGROL SHER GANG 'GRO, RGYAL DU LHA MOR BSKANG BA
'BUM DANG GZHAN RNAMS LA STONG RTZA, RNAM

RGYAL GRA TSANG NAS GRA PA GRANGS BCAD KYIS MDOS SNA KHA YAR,
RDO LHA MA nI SPYAN 'BYED, RDZONG GZHIS NYI SHUR

SNGAGS BON GYI DGRA LHA DBANGS BSTOD, LHA SAR NGAN LONG MANG BAR
SBYIN GTONG, BRTAN BZHUGS 'BUL

BAR PHEBS PA'I GRA TSANG KHAG RNAMS KYIS LHA SAR GDUGS DKAR CHIG
'BUM BRGYAD KHRI BDUN STONG DGU

BRGYA LNGA BCU, GSER 'OD CHIG STONG GYA DRUG ,CHA GSUM BRGYA
DANG SO GSUM, GZHIS RTZER NGOR BA BRGYAS

ZLA GCIG BAR RNAM 'JOMS GANG 'GRO SGROGS SHING, RANG BYON LNGA
LDAN GYI DRUNG DU TSER GSEB PA'I BTZUN

MAS YIG DRUG SA YA BZHI DANG NYIS 'BUM (67BA) BZHI KHRI, BRGYA
MCHOD, MYUR PHEBS SU MI SER KHAG

SBYONG CHE BAR GSHOR KHAL GNYIS RE'I 'GYED, RIN SPUNGS DANG
'PHYONG RGYAS SU SNGAGS BON RNAMS KYIS YE

'BROG BRGYAD CU'I BZLOG PA, NOR BU 'OD 'BAR, GSHIN RJE'I TSANG
BZLOG RDZONG GZHIS BDUN CU SKOR

NAS LAM BCOS, DBUS GTZANG GI RDZONG GZHIS BCO LNGAR DGRA LHA
DBANGS BSTOD RNAMS, NGEDo KYIo RIM

GROR LHA SA DANG GONG DKAR GYIS GTZOS RDZONG GZHIS BCU GCIG TU
DGE DGON 'BREL MTSUNGS NAS GRA PA

BRGYA RES KHYON 'BUM TSAR DGU BRGYA GO GNYIS, GSER 'OD NYIS
STONG, THANG YIG DRUG BRGYA SUM CU,

GDUGS DKAR CHIG 'BUM CHIG KHRI SUM STONG BZHI BRGYA ZHE BRGYAD,
SHER SNYING SUM 'BUM NYIS KHRI BRGYAD

ZLA BA DGU PA'I TSESo BDUN LA DPON

MO AA NU DHA RAS 'BUL YON SBYAR BA'I RNAM RGYAL GRA TSANG GIS
GZIMS CHUNG BRTAN BZHUGS DANG, TSESo

BRGYAD LA BSAM YAS CHOS SKYONG GIS MKHAN TSANG SLOB DPON BLO
BZANG THABS MKHAS DANG SKU RTEN

MNGAGS TE 'BUL YON SBYAR NAS RNAM RGYAL GRA TSANG GIS GZIMS
CHUNG BRTAN BZHUGS PHUL, GONG DKAR

BSHAD SGRUB GLING GI GRA PA BSTAN PA CHOS 'PHEL GYIS DBU MA THEG
CHEN RGYA MTSOR 'JUG PA'I GRU RDZINGS RTZA

BA DANG BCAS PA'I RGYUGS PHUL,

TSESo BCU GCIG LA GTING SKYES LHA SDE MI SDE DANG, GLEGS BAM RIN
PO CHE NAS GNAS DANG GANG

ZAG LUNG RGYAS PAR BSTAN PA RJE BLA MA'I YANG SRID GONG MA DGE
BSNYEN CHOS 'PHEL LAM 'BROM STON RGYAL

BA'I 'BYUNG GNAS KYIS RAB BYUNG DANG PO'I ME BYA LA BTAB PA'I
RVA SGRENG RGYAL BA'I DBEN (122NA) GNAS

KYI BLA MA SPYI SO DAN BCAS PAS RTA BCU GCIG SOGS KYI 'BUL YON
DANG, TSES BCU GNYIS LA PHA BONG KHA

ZHAL SNGA NAS 'JAM DBYANGS GRAGS PA'I DBON PO RAB 'BYAMS PA BLO
BZANG THABS MKHAS KYIS 'BUL

YON SBYAR BA'I RNAM RGYAL GRA TSANG NAS GZIMS CHUNG BRTAN BZHUGS
PHUL, DE MTSAMS BSAM YAS CHOS

SKYONG CHEN POR 'BUL RGYU'I SKU CHAS RGYAS PA DING PHON HOR SOGS
GOS BZANG BSGRIGS LAS GRUB PA CHA

'GRIG LA PHYAG NAS GNANG TSUL BYAS, TSES BCU GSUM LA PHA BONG
KHA ZHAL SNGA NAS NGAG DBANG BSTAN

'DZIN GYIS BDAG CAG GI STON PA THUB PA'I DBANG PO DANG, RJE BLA
MA SRID ZHI'I GTZUG RGYAN DAM PA'I SKU

BRNYAN GSER ZANGS LAS GRUB PA BZHENGS PA'I SMON LAM DANG, RNAM
RGYAL GRA TSANG GI GRA PA PA SPE SKYA BA

NGAG DBANG TSUL KHRIMS DANG, 'PHYONG RGYAS PA SNGAGS RAMS BLO
BZANG THUGS RJE, GNYAL PA DKON COG

NGAG DBANG GSUM GYIS DKON GNYER 'JOG TU DNGUL GYI BYA MA BUM CHA
DANG, ZHABS BRTAN THOG GRA TSANG

DU KHRO'I ME DAM CHA 'BUL RGYU'I BKA' RTZOM RNAMS GNANG TSUL DU
SONG, THANG LHA DANG CHOS SKYONG CHEN PO

SOGS KYI GO GSOL RGYAS PA'ANG BSTAR, 'DI NYIN RNAM RGYAL GRA
TSANG GI GRA PA RDO PA PHYAG RDOR DBANG PHYUG

@161

GIS RDO RJE SLOB DPON BYAS PA'I RGYAL RDZONGS DANG, BKA' 'GYUR
KHANG DU 'BRAS SPUNGS BDE YANGS KYI GRA

PA BRGYAS RJE BLA MA'I DGONGS RDZOGS SU DMIGS BCO LNGA GNAM GANG

DE PHYIN BKA' 'GYUR TSAR BCU GNYIS SGROG (122BA)PA'I 'GO TSUGS,

PHYI DANG LUNG LAS KYI 'JA' SA

BLA MA SRID ZHI'I GTZUG RGYAN GYI RANG

BSTAN LA DAD ZHEN THUN MONG MA YIN YANG SPRUL SKU GONG MA GSHEGS
RJES MA MA BZHENGS PA'I BAR DBON

PO BSOD NAMS NOR BU HA CANG RGYAS BSDUS MED PA DPA' THAL GYIS
RKYEN BYAS, BLO BSAM LA YANG GDON

ZHUGS LTA BUR SNANG BAR SPRUL SKU'I ZHABS 'DREN DU SONG NA'ANG
DBON PO RANG LA LCAGS BYA LO RTZAD GCOD

MI BYED THU MED DANG, PHUGS YUL YANG PHYAG PHYI 'DRAS SPRUL
SKU'I ZHABS 'DREN DU SONG DOGS PA'I SA

RIGS 'OS 'TSAMS LAS SPRUL PA'I SKUR 'PHRAL YUN TSANG MAR PHAN
SLEBS CHE BA'I BDAG RKYEN GYIS PHYAG

MDZOD DU DBON PO DON RIN PAS MTSO GZHUNG NAS BSKO BZHAG DANG,
MCHOD GZHIS KONG PO DE MO KHUL DU

PHYED SUM BRGYA SKOR DANG RDZI THO DGON MA LAG ,RDZI THO'I MI
SER THOG KHYUNG PO BSNAN PA'I DUD CHE CHUNG LNGA

BRGYA RE BZHI SKOR GYI RKANG 'GRO LAG 'DON LHO BOD BLA CHEN DPE
'GRE DGOS PA SOGS KYI BKOD PA SONG,

TSESo BCOo LNGAR THUGS SRAS ZLA BA DANG, CHOS RJE BKRA BZANG PA
GNYIS KYI 'BUL BA BSTAR, TSES

TSOGS BLA MA DANG, YE SHES DGE SLONG CAN 'GRUL SDEBS DANG BCAS
PAS GZIMS CHUNG KHAMS GSUM DU

'BUL BA BSTAR ZHING BKA' SHOG RTEN SGRAGS PHUL, PAGS RAS NGAG
(123NA)DON CAN GYIS RTA SUM CU

SO GCIG DANG JO RIG THU TSE RING CAN YUM SRAS KYIS RTA BCU RNAMS

NAS BDUN GCIG GI BAR TSE DPAG

TSUL DANG, NYER GCIG LA JO RDZONG

KHUL DU'ANG DOGS GZHI MANG BA BYUNG BA'I LI THANG DGON LAG BZHAG
SAR DU'ANG BLA MA LHA DBANG CHOS

'BYOR GYI SBYIN BDAG ZHIG TU BUD MED DE KHAR LHA MO LTA BU ZHUGS
NAS 'JAM DBYANGS SAM SPYAN RAS

GZIGS KYI SPRUL BA SKYE PA'I LUNG BSTAN TSUL DANG BCAS PHA BONG
KHA 'JAM DBYANGS GRAGS PA'I SKYE BA

'BYUNG BAR DOGS PA'I KHUNGS KYI YI GE SOGS BYUNG BAR RJES MA
RTZAD BCAD PAS ZLA BA BDUN SONG NAS

MNGAL NAS SHOR BA SHA KHRAG SOGS MIN PA'I 'O MA 'DRA BA'I DKAR
PO DE 'DRA DON BYUNG, DA DUNG LHA

MO'AM 'DRE DE PHEBS NAS 'ONG BA YOD ZER BYUNG ZER BA SOGS RDZUN
GYI TSIG JI SNYED BYUNG, RGYAL RTZE KHUL

CHU LHO BYANG STOD SMAD KYI ZAM PA ZHIG GSO'I RDO SHING BZO BO
PHOGS GLA 'U LAG GI GLA LTO'I RTZIS SHING CHA'I RI

GONG BCAS 'BRUR PHAB RU'I CHIG STONG BRGYAD BRGYA DGU BCU GO
GCIG BRE BCU GSUM PHUL PHYED BZHI,

GZHIS RTZE KHUL LHUN PO RTZE'I ZAM PA ZHO (152BA) LNGA LA TSUN
GYI ZAM PA LE TSAN BZHI, RTA NAG LCAGS ZAM

ZHIG GSO, GZHIS RTZE ZAM CHEN GYI RU 'DZIN ZHIG GSO, RTA NAG LAM
CHEN ZAM PA PHU CHUS DMIGS MED

DU KHYER BA'I GSAR BZOS BCAS KYI LAS RGYAB, RDO SHING BZO BO
PHOGS GLA, 'U LAG GI GLA LTO'I RTZIS,

SHING CHA'I RI GONG BCAS 'BRUR PHAB KHAL DRUG BRGYA NYI SHU RTZA
DRUG BRE DO PHUL DO, SNE'U SDONG YAR STOD KHUL

SHAM PO ZAM PAS GTZOS PA'I ZAM BZO'I 'U LAG GI GLA LTO SHING
CHA'I RI GONG BCAS 'BRUR PHAB RU'I KHAL

CHIG STONG BRGYA DANG DGU BRE BCU GSUM PHUL LNGA, GONG DKAR KHUL
SKYID SHONGS GRAGS CHEN, GRA NANG SPYI

STOD SMAD BAR GSUM GYI ZAM PA GSAR BZO'I 'U LAG GI GLA LTO'I
SHING CHA'I RI GONG BCAS 'BRUR PHAB

RU'I KHAL BRGYA DANG NGA BDUN BRE LNGA, RIN SPUNGS KHUL BYAMS
CHEN, SHA RA LCAGS RDUR, NUB ZAM PA RONG

STOD STAG GRU TSUN, RI BO CHE MAN, RONG CHUNG THEM PA DKAR PO
YAN GYI ZAM BZO'I RDO SHING BZO 'U LAG

@201

BCAS KYI GLA LTO'I RTZIS SHING CHA'I RI GONG BCAS 'BRUR PHAB

RNAMS BSTAR,

TSES BCU BDUN LA GONG GI MI SNA RAB 'BYAMS PA CHOS 'BYOR DANG,

PA'I SA BCAD BYAS, STON MO

BCAS PAS SO SO'I SGER 'BUL

KYANG BSTAR, SGER RGYAS G-YUL RGYAL GYI BSNGO RTEN DU RTA BZHI
BCU ZHE GSUM DANG, NAG CHUR SEMS DPA'I

SHOG KHRO DAR GYI GSON BSNGO RTEN RTA BCU RNAMS PHUL, PA RA
BYANG KI MA PAS HA RANG GNYIS DANG, BU MO

CHUNG NGU LO GSUM 'GRO BA BCAS PA TSE RING BA'I SHIS BRJOD BKA'
RTZOM TSUL DU SONG, DE NUB NAS YANG

GSANG DRAG PO'I SKU MTSAMS GNANG TSUL, CHOS SKYONG CHEN PO'I
GSUNG BZHIN YUL GRU THAMS CAD NAS LHA

MO'I BSKANG BA DANG, MA MDOS RGYAS PA, NGEDo RANGo LA NA CHAGS
LTA BU'I CUNG 'TSUB PA BZLOG THABS SU,

SHEL DKAR DU CHOS SDE BA, RIN SPUNGS SU BYAMS CHEN PA, LHA PHUR
DGE DGON TSO BSDUS RNAMS KYIS

GDUGS DKAR SUM 'BUM CHIG KHRI LNGA STONG, CHOS SKYONG GI GSUNG
BZHIN SNE'U SDONG DU DAR GLING RI CHOS

BSGRIL BAS MTSAN BRJOD TSAR CHIG 'BUM SUM KHRI TSIG STONG DGU
BRGYA, SER 'BRAS DGE GSUM LA

DNGUL 'GYED DANG JA TSUL LNGA BCU RER GDUGS DKAR DRUG 'BUM SUM
KHRI NYIS BRGYA, SHER SNYING SA YA

YA GCIG DANG DRUG 'BUM, NGEDo RANGo

SKYED CHUNG ZHING LO SNGON MA NAS MGOR BYA

KYI STOBS SHOR BA SOGS DNGOS

DANG RMI LAM DER (153BA) MA ZAD PHYI'I LTAS KYANG BZANG RGYU MA
BYUNG ZHING, RANG SEMS SU RJEo BLAo MAo SRIDo

ZHI'Io GTZUGo RGYAN GYI DGONGS PA RDZOGS PA'I CHED RTEN BZHENGS
KYI DBUS PA SOGS MA RDZOGS PA DANG,

SLAR YANG ZHING 'DIR BRTZE BAS PHEBS PA MCHOGo GIo SPRUL PA'Io
